# Pokémon Shattered Crowns: Complete Story Bible
*Includes full dialogue summaries and quest details.*


# Source: Main_Story.rb


## Act 1: NORMAL LIFE (Chapters 1-8)


### Chapter 1: Home - Dawnhaven Village

#### Scene: Chapter 1 wake up (`ch1_wake_up`)
- **Mom**: \Player! Time to wake up!  
- **Mom**: Professor Aldric is waiting for you at the lab!  
- **Mom**: Today's the day you get your first Pokémon!  
> *You stretched and looked around your room in Dawnhaven Village.*  
> *The morning sun lived up to the town's name.*  
> *Today was finally the day...*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 morning routine (`ch1_morning_routine`)
> *You took a moment to look around your room.*  
> *Posters of Champion battles. Model Pokéballs. A worn map.*  
- **\Player**: (I've been waiting for this day my whole life.)  
- **\Player**: (Today... everything changes.)  
> *You got dressed quickly.*  
> *Your adventure clothes. Chosen weeks ago.*  
> *Finally, you were going to use them.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 breakfast with family (`ch1_breakfast_with_family`)
> *The kitchen was lively this morning.*  
> *Mom had maps spread across the table between breakfast plates.*  
> *Dad was polishing an old Pokéball.*  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: Eat up! Can't start an adventure on an empty stomach!  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Your mother's right. Trust me.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: I learned that the hard way in my Champion days.  
- **\Player**: Dad, you've told that story a hundred times.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: And I'll tell it a hundred more!  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: *rolling eyes* Here we go...  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Elite Four, final battle. I was starving.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Almost lost because my stomach growled louder than my Charizard!  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: That's not quite how I remember it.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Artistic license, dear.  
> *You laughed. Your parents were ridiculous.*  
> *But you wouldn't have it any other way.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 dad gift (`ch1_dad_gift`)
- **Dad (Marcus)**: \Player. Before you go.  
> *He pulled out a worn Pokéball.*  
> *His hands were scarred. Battle-worn.*  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: This was my first partner's child.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Raised her myself after the egg hatched.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: She insisted on going with you.  
- **\Player**: Dad... I can't take—  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: You can. And you will.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: I was Champion once. Your mother saved the world with me.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Twice.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: *from the kitchen* Three times if you count the Hoenn incident!  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: *smiling* The point is...  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: We won't hold you back. This is YOUR journey.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: But when you need us... we'll be there.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: Always.  
> *You hugged them both.*  
> *The best parents a trainer could ask for.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 walk to lab (`ch1_walk_to_lab`)
> *Dawnhaven Village was peaceful in the morning light.*  
> *Neighbors waved as you passed.*  
- **Old Man**: Off to get your starter, \Player?  
- **Old Man**: Good luck out there!  
- **Young Girl**: Mommy, mommy! \Player's gonna be a trainer!  
- **Mother**: Maybe someday you will too, dear.  
> *You'd lived in this village your whole life.*  
> *Everyone knew everyone.*  
> *But today... today you'd finally see what was beyond.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 village memories (`ch1_village_memories`)
> *You passed the old oak tree where you used to play.*  
> *The pond where wild Magikarp splashed.*  
> *The fields where Mareep grazed peacefully.*  
- **\Player**: (I'm going to miss this place...)  
> *But the world was calling.*  
> *And you couldn't ignore it anymore.*  
> *The Professor's lab rose ahead.*  
> *Your heart pounded with anticipation.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 ragnar appears (`ch1_ragnar_appears`)
- **Ragnar**: YO! \Player! WAIT UP!  
> *A familiar voice echoed across the village.*  
> *You turned to see your childhood friend sprinting toward you.*  
> *Ragnar. Your neighbor. Your rival since you could walk.*  
> *Competitive. Loud. Loyal to a fault.*  
- **Ragnar**: *panting* You weren't... gonna leave... without me!  
- **\Player**: I was just getting a head start.  
- **Ragnar**: HA! Classic \Player!  
- **Ragnar**: Always trying to be first!  
- **Ragnar**: Well NOT TODAY!  
> *He grinned, that same competitive spark in his eyes.*  
> *You'd been racing each other your whole lives.*  
> *Why would today be any different?*  
- **Ragnar**: Let's go get our starters TOGETHER!  
- **Ragnar**: And then I'll beat you in our first battle!  
- **\Player**: We'll see about that.  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 lab arrival (`ch1_lab_arrival`)
> *The Professor's lab was a modest building.*  
> *But inside, it was filled with wonders.*  
> *Shelves of ancient artifacts. Glowing machines.*  
> *And in the center... three Pokéballs.*  
- **Ragnar**: Whoa... so cool...  
- **Professor Aldric**: Ah! Right on time!  
- **Professor Aldric**: Both of you! Come in, come in!  
> *The Professor was an older man with kind eyes.*  
> *Silver hair and a warm smile.*  
> *He'd known your father. They'd been friends.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 professor talk (`ch1_professor_talk`)
- **Professor Aldric**: Before we begin...  
- **Professor Aldric**: I want you to understand something.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Being a trainer isn't just about battles.  
- **Professor Aldric**: It's about partnership. Trust. Friendship.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Your Pokémon will be your companion.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Through good times and bad.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Treat them with respect.  
- **\Player**: I understand, Professor.  
- **Professor Aldric**: *nodding* Good.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Your father understood that too.  
- **Professor Aldric**: You have his spirit.  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 get starter (`ch1_get_starter`)
- **Professor Aldric**: Ah, \Player! Perfect timing!  
- **Professor Aldric**: I have three Pokémon here, each one special.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Choose wisely - this partner will be with you forever.  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 starter bond (`ch1_starter_bond`)
> *The Pokéball opened...*  
> *And there it was. Your first Pokémon.*  
> *It looked up at you with curious eyes.*  
> *Then... a happy cry.*  
- **\Player**: Hey there, partner.  
- **\Player**: Looks like we're going to be together for a long time.  
> *You knelt down and extended your hand.*  
> *Your starter sniffed it...*  
> *Then nuzzled against you affectionately.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: *smiling* A perfect match.  
- **Professor Aldric**: I knew it would be.  
> *Something clicked in that moment.*  
> *Like two puzzle pieces finding each other.*  
> *You'd found your partner.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 ragnar starter (`ch1_ragnar_starter`)
- **Ragnar**: Okay, my turn! MY TURN!  
> *Ragnar bounced on his heels excitedly.*  
> *He reached for a Pokéball with barely contained energy.*  
- **Ragnar**: This one! I can feel it!  
> *The ball opened, revealing a Pikachu.*  
> *The electric mouse sparked with energy.*  
- **Ragnar**: PERFECT! A Pikachu!  
- **Ragnar**: We're gonna be UNSTOPPABLE!  
- **Pikachu**: Pika!  
> *The Pikachu immediately climbed onto Ragnar's shoulder.*  
> *They were a perfect match too.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: *chuckling* Two excellent pairs.  
- **Professor Aldric**: I expect great things from both of you.  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 first rival battle (`ch1_first_rival_battle`)
> *Outside the lab, Ragnar blocked your path.*  
> *That competitive grin on his face.*  
- **Ragnar**: Hey \Player!  
- **Ragnar**: We've got our partners now...  
- **Ragnar**: So there's only ONE thing to do!  
- **\Player**: You want to battle already?  
- **Ragnar**: DUH!  
- **Ragnar**: We've been waiting our whole lives for this!  
- **Ragnar**: First one to beat the other STARTS with the advantage!  
- **Pikachu**: Pika pika!  
> *Your starter stepped forward, ready.*  
- **\Player**: You're on, Ragnar.  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 after rival battle (`ch1_after_rival_battle`)
- **Ragnar**: *laughing* Man, that was AWESOME!  
- **Ragnar**: Win or lose, that was our first real battle!  
- **\Player**: It was a good fight.  
- **Ragnar**: This is just the beginning, \Player!  
- **Ragnar**: By the time we reach the Pokémon League...  
- **Ragnar**: I'll be WAY stronger!  
- **\Player**: We'll see about that.  
- **Ragnar**: *grinning* That's the spirit!  
- **Ragnar**: Catch you later, rival!  
> *Ragnar took off down a different path.*  
> *His Pikachu clinging to his shoulder.*  
- **\Player**: (Same old Ragnar...)  
- **\Player**: (But I wouldn't have it any other way.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 receive pokedex (`ch1_receive_pokedex`)
- **Professor Aldric**: One more thing before you go.  
> *He handed you a sleek red device.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: This is the Pokédex.  
- **Professor Aldric**: It records data on every Pokémon you encounter.  
- **Professor Aldric**: I'd appreciate it if you could help complete it.  
- **\Player**: Leave it to me, Professor!  
- **Professor Aldric**: I'm also giving you these Pokéballs.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Use them to catch wild Pokémon.  
> *You received 5 Pokéballs!*  
- **Professor Aldric**: Now go, \Player.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Your adventure awaits!  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 parents goodbye (`ch1_parents_goodbye`)
> *Both your parents met you at the village gate.*  
> *Dad had his old adventure bag. Mom had her research notes.*  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: I packed some supplies.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: Potions, berries, and my field notes on local Pokémon.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: And I put in some battle tips.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: Learned a few things as Champion.  
- **\Player**: You two are the best.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: *hugging you* We're proud of you already.  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: *joining the hug* Go show them what our kid can do.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: And remember...  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: When you need us...  
- **Both**: We'll be there.  
- **Ragnar**: *waving from down the road* SEE YA AT THE GYM, \Player!  
- **Ragnar**: DON'T KEEP ME WAITING!  
- **Dad (Marcus)**: *chuckling* That kid has energy.  
- **Mom (Aurora)**: Good. \Player will need a rival to push them.  
> *With a final wave, you stepped beyond the village gate.*  
> *Your parents watched, arms around each other.*  
> *The road stretched ahead.*  
> *Your adventure had begun.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 first wild battle (`ch1_first_wild_battle`)
> *Not far from the village, rustling in the grass!*  
> *A wild Rattata appeared!*  
- **\Player**: This is it! Our first battle!  
- **\Player**: Let's go, partner!  
> *Your starter leaped forward eagerly.*  
> *The battle was short but fierce.*  
> *Victory!*  
- **\Player**: Great job! You're amazing!  
> *Your starter puffed up with pride.*  
> *This was just the beginning.*  
> *But it felt like the start of something incredible.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 strange dream (`ch1_strange_dream`)
> *That night, you had a strange dream...*  
> *Golden light. Fragments of something broken.*  
> *A voice, barely a whisper...*  
> *\\ts[]'Soon...'*  
> *You woke with a start.*  
> *(What was that...?)*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 dream details (`ch1_dream_details`)
> *You tried to remember the dream.*  
> *Fragments of images...*  
> *A crown. Broken into pieces.*  
> *Three figures standing against darkness.*  
> *And a roar... ancient and terrible.*  
- **\Player**: (What does it mean?)  
> *Your starter nuzzled against you.*  
> *As if sensing your unease.*  
- **\Player**: *petting* It's okay, buddy.  
- **\Player**: Probably just a weird dream.  
> *But somehow... you didn't believe that.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 1 route exploration (`ch1_route_exploration`)
> *The next morning, you set out on Route 1.*  
> *The path wound through gentle hills and forests.*  
> *Wild Pokémon watched from the bushes.*  
> *Birds sang in the trees.*  
> *Everything felt fresh and new.*  
- **\Player**: The world is so big...  
- **\Player**: I can't wait to see all of it.  
> *Your starter bounded ahead.*  
> *Just as excited as you were.*  
> *Ahead, you could see a farm in the distance.*  
> *Sunrise Farm. Your first destination.*  


### Chapter 2: Reunion - Sunrise Farm & Meeting Kael

#### Scene: Chapter 2 farm arrival (`ch2_farm_arrival`)
> *Sunrise Farm appeared over the hill.*  
> *Rolling fields of berries. Grazing Miltank.*  
> *The scent of fresh earth and flowers.*  
- **\Player**: This must be the place.  
- **\Player**: Lyra said to meet her here.  
> *A figure waved from the farmhouse.*  
> *Bright smile. Boundless energy.*  
> *That had to be Lyra.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 meet lyra (`ch2_meet_lyra`)
- **Lyra**: \Player! Over here!  
> *A cheerful girl waved from Sunrise Farm.*  
> *The berry fields stretched behind her, vibrant and alive.*  
> *Beside her stood a small Eevee.*  
- **Lyra**: This is Willow! Grandma gave her to me.  
- **Lyra**: She's a little shy, but she's the sweetest!  
- **Willow**: Vee...  
- **\Player**: She's adorable! Nice to meet you, Willow.  
- **Lyra**: Hey, did you have any weird dreams last night?  
- **Lyra**: I had this strange dream about golden light...  
- **\Player**: Wait... me too. Golden light and broken pieces.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 pokemon introductions (`ch2_pokemon_introductions`)
> *Your starter and Willow sniffed each other curiously.*  
> *Then they started playing!*  
- **Lyra**: Aww! They're already friends!  
- **Willow**: Vee vee!  
- **\Player**: Looks like they get along.  
- **Lyra**: Pokémon are good judges of character.  
- **Lyra**: If Willow likes your partner...  
- **Lyra**: Then you must be a good person!  
- **\Player**: *laughing* I hope so.  
> *The two Pokémon chased each other through the berry bushes.*  
> *Carefree. Happy. Like you wished you could be.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 ragnar route (`ch2_ragnar_route`)
> *A familiar voice echoed across the route.*  
- **Ragnar**: YO! \Player! OVER HERE!  
> *Ragnar was sitting by a tree, Pikachu on his shoulder.*  
> *A Rattata and a Pidgey sat nearby.*  
- **\Player**: Ragnar? You're ahead of me already?  
- **Ragnar**: Duh! I've been training non-stop!  
- **Ragnar**: Already caught two new partners!  
- **Ragnar**: How many have YOU caught?  
- **\Player**: I'm... taking my time.  
- **Ragnar**: HA! Classic Broody!  
- **Ragnar**: Always overthinking everything!  
> *His Pikachu sparked playfully at your starter.*  
- **Ragnar**: Don't worry, I'll wait for you at the first Gym!  
- **Ragnar**: So I can watch you TRY to catch up!  
> *He took off running, laughing.*  
> *Some things never change.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 farm tour (`ch2_farm_tour`)
- **Lyra**: Let me show you around!  
> *She led you through the berry fields.*  
> *Cheri, Pecha, Oran... every variety.*  
- **Lyra**: We grow berries for the whole region!  
- **Lyra**: Grandma started this farm 40 years ago.  
- **\Player**: It's amazing. So peaceful.  
- **Lyra**: I love it here. But...  
- **Lyra**: I've always wanted to see more.  
> *You helped water some plants.*  
> *Fed the Miltank.*  
> *Chased a runaway Wooloo.*  
- **Lyra**: *laughing* Watch out for—  
> *The Wooloo knocked you over.*  
- **Lyra**: —that one. Sorry!  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 lyra backstory (`ch2_lyra_backstory`)
> *You walked through the berry fields with Lyra.*  
> *The afternoon sun painted everything golden.*  
- **Lyra**: I've always loved this farm.  
- **Lyra**: My parents... they're always traveling for work.  
- **Lyra**: But Grandma's always here.  
- **\Player**: That sounds nice. A real home.  
- **Lyra**: It is! And now with Willow, I'm never lonely.  
- **Willow**: Vee vee!  
- **Lyra**: I want to become a Pokémon Nurse someday.  
- **Lyra**: Help all the injured Pokémon I can.  
- **\Player**: That's a wonderful dream.  
- **Lyra**: What about you? What do you want to be?  
- **\Player**: Honestly? I just want to explore.  
- **\Player**: See everything the world has to offer.  
- **Lyra**: Then let's go on adventures together!  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 lyra sister mention (`ch2_lyra_sister_mention`)
- **Lyra**: Oh! I should tell you about my sister!  
- **Lyra**: Her name's Elena. She's amazing.  
- **\Player**: Where is she?  
- **Lyra**: Traveling, like my parents.  
- **Lyra**: She's a researcher. Studies ancient legends.  
- **Lyra**: *proudly* She sends me letters from everywhere!  
- **Lyra**: The Eternal Forest. The Crown Mountains.  
- **Lyra**: She's seen it all.  
- **\Player**: She sounds brave.  
- **Lyra**: She is! I want to be just like her someday.  
- **Lyra**: Maybe we'll run into her on our journey!  
> *(Little did you know how important that meeting would be.)*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 sunset talk (`ch2_sunset_talk`)
> *You sat on the fence, watching the sunset.*  
> *Orange and pink painted the sky.*  
- **Lyra**: Beautiful, isn't it?  
- **\Player**: Yeah... really beautiful.  
- **Lyra**: My parents used to watch sunsets with me.  
- **Lyra**: Before they started traveling all the time.  
- **\Player**: Do you miss them?  
- **Lyra**: *quietly* Every day.  
- **Lyra**: But Grandma says they're doing important work.  
- **Lyra**: Research that could help everyone.  
- **\Player**: My dad was Champion once.  
- **\Player**: He and my mom still go on adventures sometimes.  
- **Lyra**: That's so cool! Champion parents!  
- **Lyra**: No wonder you want to explore!  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 grandmother warning (`ch2_grandmother_warning`)
> *Lyra's grandmother watched from the porch.*  
> *Something in her eyes seemed... knowing.*  
- **Grandmother**: You must be \Player.  
- **Grandmother**: Lyra's told me all about you.  
- **\Player**: It's nice to meet you, ma'am.  
- **Grandmother**: *studying you* Hmm...  
- **Grandmother**: You have old eyes for someone so young.  
- **\Player**: I... do?  
- **Grandmother**: Take care of each other out there.  
- **Grandmother**: The world is changing.  
- **Grandmother**: And something tells me... you'll be at the center of it.  
- **Lyra**: Grandma! Stop being cryptic!  
- **Grandmother**: *laughs* Go on, you two. Have fun.  
> *(Strange... what did she mean?)*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 grandmother stories (`ch2_grandmother_stories`)
> *That night, Grandmother told stories by the fire.*  
- **Grandmother**: Long ago, this region was protected.  
- **Grandmother**: By three great guardians.  
- **Lyra**: The crown story again?  
- **Grandmother**: It's important, child.  
- **Grandmother**: They say the guardians sleep now.  
- **Grandmother**: Waiting for those worthy to awaken them.  
- **\Player**: Who would be worthy?  
- **Grandmother**: *mysterious smile* Those with pure hearts.  
- **Grandmother**: Those willing to sacrifice for others.  
- **Grandmother**: Those who forge unbreakable bonds.  
> *The fire crackled.*  
> *For a moment, you could have sworn you saw shapes in the flames.*  
> *A wolf. A deer. A great bird.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 shared dream (`ch2_shared_dream`)
> *That night, you dreamed again.*  
> *The same dream. Golden light.*  
> *But this time... you weren't alone.*  
> *Lyra was there. And a third figure, shrouded in shadow.*  
> *\\ts[]'Three must stand...'*  
> *\\ts[]'Against the coming dark...'*  
> *You woke to find Lyra already awake.*  
> *Eyes wide.*  
- **Lyra**: You had the dream too, didn't you?  
- **\Player**: The same one. With you in it.  
- **Lyra**: And someone else...  
- **Lyra**: Who was the third person?  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 departure farm (`ch2_departure_farm`)
> *Morning came. Time to continue your journey.*  
- **Grandmother**: Take care of my granddaughter.  
- **\Player**: I will. I promise.  
- **Lyra**: Grandma, don't worry! I can take care of myself!  
- **Grandmother**: I know, dear. But it's nice to have friends.  
> *She pressed something into Lyra's hands.*  
> *A small pendant. Shaped like leaves.*  
- **Grandmother**: This belonged to your mother.  
- **Grandmother**: Keep it close.  
- **Lyra**: *hugging her* I love you, Grandma.  
- **Grandmother**: Go make me proud.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 road to shadowfen (`ch2_road_to_shadowfen`)
> *You traveled through Willowmere.*  
> *A peaceful village by a lake.*  
- **Lyra**: I've heard there's someone else in Shadowfen.  
- **Lyra**: Another trainer our age.  
- **\Player**: Friend of yours?  
- **Lyra**: Not exactly... we've exchanged letters.  
- **Lyra**: He's... intense.  
- **\Player**: Intense how?  
- **Lyra**: You'll see.  
> *The path ahead led into darker woods.*  
> *Shadowfen was close.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 shadowfen arrival (`ch2_shadowfen_arrival`)
> *Shadowfen lived up to its name.*  
> *Twisted trees. Murky water. Eerie silence.*  
- **Lyra**: *shivering* This place is creepy...  
- **Willow**: Vee...  
- **\Player**: Stay close. We don't know what's out there.  
> *Fog rolled between the trees.*  
> *Something moved in the shadows.*  
> *But it wasn't attacking. Just... watching.*  
- **Lyra**: The library ruins should be up ahead.  
- **Lyra**: That's where Kael said he'd be.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 meet kael (`ch2_meet_kael`)
> *You traveled through Willowmere and into Shadowfen.*  
> *The swamp village was eerie, but beyond it lay the old library ruins.*  
> *You found Kael there, reading alone. A Zorua at his feet.*  
- **Kael**: ...You're late.  
- **Lyra**: Nice to see you too, grumpy!  
- **Kael**: ...  
> *His Zorua, Shadow, eyed you suspiciously.*  
- **Kael**: I heard you both had strange dreams.  
- **Kael**: So did I. The same one.  
- **Kael**: That's... statistically improbable.  
- **\Player**: Three of us having the exact same dream? That's not coincidence.  
- **\Player**: Something's going on.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 kael introduction (`ch2_kael_introduction`)
> *Kael was different from Lyra.*  
> *Cold where she was warm. Quiet where she was loud.*  
- **Lyra**: Kael, this is \Player!  
- **Kael**: I know. You mentioned them in your letters.  
- **\Player**: Nice to meet you.  
- **Kael**: Hmm.  
> *Shadow circled you suspiciously.*  
> *Then seemed to relax.*  
- **Kael**: Shadow approves. That's... rare.  
- **Lyra**: See? \Player's great!  
- **Kael**: We'll see.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 kael backstory (`ch2_kael_backstory`)
> *You tried to get to know Kael better.*  
> *It wasn't easy. He deflected most questions.*  
- **Lyra**: So where are you from, Kael?  
- **Kael**: Nowhere.  
- **Lyra**: Everyone's from somewhere!  
- **Kael**: I grew up in an orphanage. It burned down.  
- **Kael**: There. Happy?  
- **Lyra**: Oh... I'm sorry, I didn't—  
- **Kael**: Don't. I don't need pity.  
> *Shadow rubbed against Kael's leg.*  
- **Kael**: Shadow was there too. We escaped together.  
- **Kael**: She's all I need.  
- **Shadow**: Zor...  
- **\Player**: Well, now you have us too.  
- **Kael**: ...We'll see.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 library exploration (`ch2_library_exploration`)
> *The library ruins were fascinating.*  
> *Ancient books. Faded murals. Forgotten knowledge.*  
- **Kael**: I've been researching the dreams.  
- **Kael**: There are references in old texts.  
- **Lyra**: What do they say?  
- **Kael**: Prophecies. Legends.  
- **Kael**: Something about 'Chosen Ones' and 'guardians.'  
- **\Player**: Like the festival story?  
- **Kael**: *surprised* You know about that?  
- **\Player**: Lyra's grandmother mentioned it.  
- **Kael**: Interesting. The old woman knows more than she lets on.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 first battle together (`ch2_first_battle_together`)
> *As you left the library, wild Pokémon blocked your path.*  
> *A territorial Nidorino and its pack.*  
- **Nidorino**: NIDO!  
- **Lyra**: They look angry!  
- **Kael**: We're in their territory. Stand back.  
- **\Player**: No. We fight together.  
- **\Player**: That's what friends do.  
- **Kael**: ...Fine. Shadow, you're up.  
- **Lyra**: Go, Willow!  
> *Your three Pokémon fought side by side.*  
> *Despite the danger, it felt... right.*  
- **Lyra**: We did it!  
- **Kael**: You weren't useless.  
- **Lyra**: Was that... a compliment?  
- **Kael**: Don't get used to it.  

#### Scene: Chapter 2 trio formed (`ch2_trio_formed`)
> *After the battle, something felt different.*  
> *A connection between the three of you.*  
- **Lyra**: We should stick together!  
- **Lyra**: We make a great team!  
- **Kael**: We barely know each other.  
- **\Player**: Then let's change that.  
- **\Player**: We're having the same dreams for a reason.  
- **\Player**: Something's bringing us together.  
- **Kael**: ...Logical.  
- **Kael**: Fine. We travel together. For now.  
- **Lyra**: *hugging them both* YAY! Best friends!  
- **Kael**: Don't touch me.  
- **Lyra**: Too late!  
> *And so, the trio was formed.*  
> *Three trainers. Three Pokémon. One destiny.*  


### Chapter 3: The Festival - Thornwood Town

#### Scene: Chapter 3 road to thornwood (`ch3_road_to_thornwood`)
> *The road to Thornwood took you through beautiful autumn forests.*  
> *Golden leaves crunched beneath your feet.*  
- **Lyra**: *skipping ahead* I love this time of year!  
- **Lyra**: The leaves, the smell, the festivals!  
- **Kael**: It's just dying vegetation.  
- **Lyra**: Way to ruin the magic, Kael.  
- **\Player**: What's special about Thornwood Town?  
- **Lyra**: It's where they hold the Festival of Crowns!  
- **Lyra**: Every year they celebrate the legend of the guardians!  
- **Kael**: Superstitious nonsense.  
- **Lyra**: You'll see! It's amazing!  
> *Shadow ran ahead, chasing falling leaves.*  
> *Even Kael smiled—just a little.*  
- **Kael**: ...Don't look at me like that.  

#### Scene: Chapter 3 thornwood entrance (`ch3_thornwood_entrance`)
> *Thornwood Town appeared through the trees.*

> *She trailed off, her smile flickering.*  
- **\Player**: Your parents?  
- **Lyra**: They... they're not around anymore.  
- **Lyra**: It's okay! That was a long time ago.  
- **Lyra**: Grandma raised me. And Elena helped too.  
- **Kael**: ...  
- **Kael**: The festival looks... adequate.  
> *Lyra beamed at him, recognizing the kindness beneath his words.*

- **Kael**: ...Adequate team.  
- **Lyra**: I'll take it!

#### Scene: Chapter 3 mask merchapter ant (`ch3_mask_merchant`)

> *The merchant said nothing more, already helping other customers.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 3 festival story (`ch3_festival_story`)
> *Thornwood Town's annual Festival of Crowns was in full swing.*  
> *Autumn leaves danced around the forest-edge town.*

- **Old Storyteller**: Let me tell you the legend of the Shattered Crowns...  
- **Old Storyteller**: Long ago, three guardians protected our world.  
- **Old Storyteller**: Each wore a crown of divine power.  
- **Old Storyteller**: But a great evil coveted their strength...  
- **Old Storyteller**: In a battle that shook the heavens...  
- **Old Storyteller**: The crowns were shattered!  
- **Lyra**: Ooh, spooky!  
- **Kael**: It's just a fairy tale.  
> *(But something about it felt... familiar.)*  

#### Scene: Chapter 3 storyteller prophecy (`ch3_storyteller_prophecy`)
> *The storyteller continued, his voice dropping low.*  
- **Old Storyteller**: But the legend doesn't end there...  
- **Old Storyteller**: The ancients spoke of a prophecy.

- **Kael**: It's a coincidence.  
> *The storyteller's eyes found yours.*  
> *For a moment, they seemed to glow with ancient knowledge.*  
- **Old Storyteller**: Perhaps. Or perhaps... the prophecy has begun.  
> *He smiled mysteriously and bowed.*  
> *When you looked for him later, he was gone.*

#### Scene: Chapter 3 ragnar festival (`ch3_ragnar_festival`)

- **Kael**: ...Maybe.

- **Lyra**: She said it was... magical.

> *Above, the real stars began to appear.*  
- **Lyra**: Elena... I wish she was here.  
- **Kael**: Where is she now?

- **Lyra**: She's always been stronger than me.  
- **\Player**: Strength isn't everything.  
- **Lyra**: *smiling* Thanks, \Player.  

#### Scene: Chapter 3 festival night (`ch3_festival_night`)

- **Kael**: ...It wasn't terrible.

- **Lyra**: She said the guardians aren't gone.  
- **Lyra**: They're sleeping. Waiting for the right people.  
- **Lyra**: 'Chosen Ones' she called them.  
- **Kael**: Fairy tales don't have 'Chosen Ones' in real life.  
- **Lyra**: Maybe not. But wouldn't it be cool?  
- **Lyra**: To be chosen for something special?  
> *You looked up at the stars.*  
> *For some reason, you couldn't shake the feeling...*  
> *That you already were.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 3 shared dream again (`ch3_shared_dream_again`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*

- **Lyra**: You heard it too?

- **Kael**: This is beyond coincidence now.  
- **Kael**: Something is deliberately contacting us.

### Chapter 4: First Signs - Wild Pokémon Acting Strange

#### Scene: Chapter 4 forest path (`ch4_forest_path`)
> *The path through Thornwood Forest was peaceful.*  
> *Dappled sunlight filtered through autumn leaves.*  
- **Lyra**: It's so pretty here!

- **Lyra**: You worry too much, Kael.  
- **\Player**: He has a point. We should stay alert.  
> *Your Pokémon walked beside you, ears perked.*  
> *Something felt different today.*  
> *The forest was quieter than usual.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 4 strange pokemon (`ch4_strange_pokemon`)
> *Something was wrong in the forest.*  
> *Wild Pokémon fled past you in panic.*  
- **Lyra**: They're terrified! What's happening?  
- **Kael**: Something's driving them out.  
- **Kael**: We should investigate.  
- **\Player**: Agreed. Let's move carefully.  

#### Scene: Chapter 4 fleeing pokemon (`ch4_fleeing_pokemon`)

- **Lyra**: It's still scared! We need to help!  
- **\Player**: We'll find the source and stop it.  
- **\Player**: Lyra, can you calm it down?

- **Lyra**: We'll protect you.

- **Lyra**: Like the air itself is sad.

- **Shadow**: Zor... zorua...

> *You gripped your Pokéball tighter.*  
> *Whatever was causing this, you'd face it together.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 4 ancient tablet (`ch4_ancient_tablet`)
> *Deep in the forest, you found the source.*  
> *An ancient stone tablet, cracked and weathered.*

> *(Strange... it's almost warm.)*

- **\Player**: He might know what it means.  

#### Scene: Chapter 4 tablet reaction (`ch4_tablet_reaction`)
> *As you touched the tablet, light flared.*  
> *Images flooded your mind—crowns, shadows, a great battle.*  
- **\Player**: Did you see that?!

- **Lyra**: I didn't see anything...  
- **Lyra**: Just felt really warm suddenly.  
- **Kael**: Interesting. Different reactions.  
- **Kael**: Perhaps we each connect to it differently.  
> *The tablet's glow faded, but the warmth remained.*  
> *Something had changed. You could feel it.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 4 pokemon returning (`ch4_pokemon_returning`)

> *Slowly, Pokémon began returning to the area.*  
- **Lyra**: Look! They're coming back!  
- **Lyra**: Whatever was scaring them... stopped.

- **Kael**: Or because something finished what it was doing?  
- **\Player**: Either way, the forest feels better now.  
> *The Caterpie from before wiggled happily.*  
- **Lyra**: *releasing it* There you go, little one!  
- **Lyra**: You're safe now!  
> *It turned back once, as if to thank you, then disappeared into the brush.*

> *A cozy forest town with the region's first Gym.*

- **Kael**: *sighing* I don't.

### Chapter 5: The Library - Kael's Research

#### Scene: Chapter 5 travel to ironvale (`ch5_travel_to_ironvale`)
> *The road to Ironvale City took you through rolling hills.*  
> *Each town you passed had stories of strange events.*  
- **Lyra**: Did you hear what that merchant said?  
- **Lyra**: 'The ground groaned last night.'  
- **Kael**: Seismic activity has increased across the region.  
- **Kael**: Something geological is happening.  
- **\Player**: Or something not-so-geological.  
- **Kael**: ...Possibly.  
> *Ironvale City appeared on the horizon.*  
> *Its famous library tower pierced the clouds.*  
- **Kael**: *eyes lighting up* The Grand Archive.  
- **Kael**: If answers exist anywhere, they're there.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 ironvale arrival (`ch5_ironvale_arrival`)
> *Ironvale City was a scholar's paradise.*  
> *Bookshops lined every street. Academics filled the cafes.*  
- **Lyra**: This place is so... intellectual.  
- **Lyra**: I feel underdressed.  
- **Kael**: For once, I feel at home.  
- **\Player**: Let's find a place to stay first.  
- **\Player**: Then you can visit your beloved library, Kael.  
- **Kael**: It's not 'beloved.' It's practical.  
- **Lyra**: Sure, Kael. Sure.  
> *Shadow bounced ahead, intrigued by all the new scents.*  
> *Even she seemed excited to explore.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 library exterior (`ch5_library_exterior`)
> *The Grand Archive was massive.*  
> *Ancient stone walls covered in ivy. Stained glass windows.*  
- **Kael**: Fifteen floors of knowledge.  
- **Kael**: Some texts here predate recorded history.  
- **Lyra**: *whistling* That's a LOT of reading.  
- **Kael**: You don't have to come.  
- **Lyra**: And miss watching you nerd out? Never!  
- **\Player**: I'm curious too.  
- **\Player**: Maybe we'll find something about those symbols.  
> *The doors creaked open, revealing endless rows of books.*  
> *The smell of old paper and knowledge filled the air.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 library researchapter  (`ch5_library_research`)
> *Kael spent three days in the old library.*  
> *Barely eating. Barely sleeping.*  
- **Lyra**: *worried* He's going to work himself to death.  
- **\Player**: That's just how Kael is.  
> *Finally, he emerged with a dusty tome.*  
- **Kael**: Found it.  
- **Kael**: The symbols on that tablet...  
- **Kael**: They mention something called 'Asgaheim.'  
- **Lyra**: Asgaheim? What's that?  
- **Kael**: I don't know. The book doesn't explain.  
- **Kael**: But it says it's 'the realm where gods sleep.'  
- **\Player**: Gods? Like... legendary Pokémon?  
- **Kael**: Maybe. Or something older.  
- **Kael**: There's more research to do.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 ancient text (`ch5_ancient_text`)
> *Kael showed you what he'd found.*  
> *An ancient text, yellowed with age.*  
- **Kael**: This book mentions 'Three Guardians.'  
- **Kael**: Beings of immense power who protected balance.  
- **Lyra**: Like the festival story!  
- **Kael**: Exactly. But this predates those stories.  
- **Kael**: This is the SOURCE.  
- **\Player**: What happened to them?  
- **Kael**: According to this...  
- **Kael**: They sacrificed themselves to seal away a great darkness.  
- **Kael**: Their power was split into 'Crown Fragments.'  
- **Kael**: Scattered across the world.  
- **Lyra**: So the shattered crowns are real...  
- **Kael**: Very real. And apparently, we're connected to them.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 librarian warning (`ch5_librarian_warning`)
> *An elderly librarian approached your table.*  
> *Her eyes were sharp despite her age.*  
- **Librarian**: You're researching the old legends.  
- **Librarian**: Be careful with that knowledge.  
- **Kael**: Why? It's just history.  
- **Librarian**: Is it?  
- **Librarian**: Some knowledge awakens things best left sleeping.  
- **Librarian**: Others have come before you. Seeking the same answers.  
- **\Player**: Others? Who?  
- **Librarian**: People in dark robes. Symbol of a broken hand.  
- **Librarian**: They took many books. Asked about the guardians.  
- **Lyra**: The Shattered Hand...  
- **Librarian**: Leave these matters alone, children.  
- **Librarian**: Before you attract their attention.  
> *She shuffled away, leaving you with a chill down your spine.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 kael revelation (`ch5_kael_revelation`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *That night, Kael couldn't sleep.*  
> *The research had awakened old memories.*  
- **Kael**: (The fire... Mira...)  
> *Shadow nuzzled his leg.*  
- **Shadow**: Zor?  
- **Kael**: I'm fine, girl.  
- **Kael**: Just... remembering.  
> *The orphanage fire. The screaming. His sister's sacrifice.*  
> *She'd pushed him out the window before the flames took her.*  
- **Kael**: I couldn't save her.  
- **Kael**: But maybe... if these legends are real...  
- **Kael**: Maybe there's power enough to prevent such things.  
> *Shadow licked his hand.*  
> *She understood. She always did.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 lyra letter (`ch5_lyra_letter`)
> *A letter arrived for Lyra from her grandmother.*  
> *Her expression grew serious as she read.*  
- **Lyra**: Grandma says Elena is coming home.  
- **Lyra**: She's been investigating something...  
- **\Player**: That's good news, right?  
- **Lyra**: I don't know. The letter sounds worried.  
- **Lyra**: Elena found something. Something about our family.  
- **Lyra**: About why we've always been connected to legends.  
- **Kael**: Another piece of the puzzle.  
- **Lyra**: I need to see her.  
- **Lyra**: She's my big sister. She always knows what to do.  
- **\Player**: We'll meet up with her. Together.  
- **Lyra**: *smiling slightly* Together.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 lyra heirloom (`ch5_lyra_heirloom`)
> *Lyra returned from visiting her grandmother.*  
> *She looked... shaken.*  
- **\Player**: Lyra? Everything okay?  
- **Lyra**: My grandmother showed me something.  
- **Lyra**: A family heirloom. Very old.  
- **Kael**: What kind of heirloom?  
- **Lyra**: A pendant. It glowed when I touched it.  
- **Lyra**: Grandma got really serious.  
- **Lyra**: She said our family has a 'duty'...  
- **Lyra**: But she wouldn't explain what.  
- **\Player**: That's strange...  
- **Kael**: Another mystery.  
- **Kael**: They're all connected. I'm sure of it.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 prophetic dream (`ch5_prophetic_dream`)
> *\\i[\Player'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *The dream was more vivid this time.*  
> *You stood in a vast chamber of light and shadow.*  
> *Three thrones. Three crowns. Three figures.*  
- **Voice**: The time of awakening draws near.  
- **Voice**: You are the bridge between worlds.  
- **Voice**: Find the fragments before the broken ones.  
- **\Player**: Who are you?! What do you want?!  
- **Voice**: We are what remains.  
- **Voice**: We are the guardians' last hope.  
- **Voice**: And you... are chosen.  
> *You woke gasping for air.*  
> *The weight of destiny felt heavier than ever.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 ragnar concern (`ch5_ragnar_concern`)
> *You were walking to meet Lyra and Kael when—*  
- **Ragnar**: *grabbing your shoulder* Hey.  
> *His usual energy was subdued.*  
- **Ragnar**: You okay? You've been... different lately.  
- **\Player**: What do you mean?  
- **Ragnar**: Quieter. More serious.  
- **Ragnar**: Those new friends of yours...  
- **Ragnar**: Something weird's going on, right?  
> *You hesitated. How much could you tell him?*  
- **\Player**: It's... complicated.  
- **Ragnar**: *crossing arms* I'm not dumb, you know.  
- **Ragnar**: I can see it in your face.  
- **Ragnar**: Whatever it is... be careful, okay?  
- **\Player**: I will.  
- **Ragnar**: Good! 'Cause I still need to beat you!  
- **Ragnar**: Can't do that if you go and disappear!  
> *He punched your shoulder lightly and jogged off.*  
> *Ragnar. Annoying but... always there.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 trio discussion (`ch5_trio_discussion`)
> *You gathered the next morning to discuss your findings.*  
> *Each of you had experienced something strange.*  
- **Kael**: The guardians. The fragments. The Shattered Hand.  
- **Kael**: It's all connected.  
- **Lyra**: And we're in the middle of it.  
- **Lyra**: Whether we like it or not.  
- **\Player**: So what do we do?  
- **Kael**: We keep moving forward.  
- **Kael**: Collect the Gym Badges. Get stronger.  
- **Kael**: And search for answers along the way.  
- **Lyra**: And stick together! No splitting up!  
- **Kael**: ...Agreed.  
- **\Player**: Then let's go. Adventure awaits.  
> *The path ahead was uncertain.*  
> *But at least you weren't walking it alone.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 earthquake (`ch5_earthquake`)
> *That night, the ground shook.*  
> *Not just here—reports came from across the region.*  
- **News Report**: Mysterious earthquakes reported...  
- **News Report**: Scientists baffled by unusual seismic patterns...  
- **Lyra**: That's the third weird thing this week!  
- **Kael**: The tablet. The heirloom. The earthquake.  
- **Kael**: Something's waking up.  
- **\Player**: What do you mean?  
- **Kael**: I don't know yet.  
- **Kael**: But whatever it is...  
- **Kael**: We're caught in the middle of it.  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 mysterious observer (`ch5_mysterious_observer`)
> *As you left the library, you felt eyes on you.*  
> *A figure watched from across the plaza.*  
- **Kael**: Don't look. But we're being watched.  
- **Lyra**: The Shattered Hand?  
- **Kael**: Possibly. Act natural.  
> *You continued walking, pretending not to notice.*  
> *The figure didn't follow—just watched.*  
- **\Player**: (Who are they? What do they want?)  
> *The sense of being hunted had begun.*  
> *Whatever game was being played, you were now pieces on the board.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 5 leaving ironvale (`ch5_leaving_ironvale`)
> *You left Ironvale City the next morning.*  
> *Armed with knowledge, but burdened by questions.*  
- **Lyra**: So we're really doing this.  
- **Lyra**: Chasing ancient legends.

- **Kael**: The legends are chasing us.  
- **\Player**: Then let's stay one step ahead.  
> *The road stretched before you.*  
> *Somewhere out there were answers.*  
> *And somewhere out there, enemies gathered.*  
> *But you were together.*  
> *And that would have to be enough.*  


### Chapter 6: Rumors - The Shattered Hand

#### Scene: Chapter 6 new city arrival (`ch6_new_city_arrival`)
> *Ashbury City sprawled before you.*  
> *A bustling metropolis of commerce and culture.*  
- **Lyra**: Wow! It's huge!  
- **Lyra**: So many people! So many shops!  
- **Kael**: And many places for enemies to hide.  
- **Lyra**: Can't you just enjoy things for once?  
- **\Player**: He has a point. Stay alert.  
- **\Player**: After what happened at the library...  
- **Lyra**: *sighing* Fine. Alert AND excited.  
> *Shadow sniffed the air suspiciously.*  
> *Even she sensed something in this city.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 cult rumors (`ch6_cult_rumors`)
> *In the city, whispers spread.*  
> *People spoke of strange figures in hoods.*  
- **Citizen**: They call themselves the Shattered Hand...  
- **Citizen**: Weird cult stuff. Stay away from them.  
- **Lyra**: Shattered Hand? Like the shattered crowns?  
- **Kael**: *eyes narrowing* Could be a coincidence.  
- **Kael**: Or could be connected to everything else.  
- **\Player**: Should we investigate?  
- **Kael**: Not yet. We don't know what we're dealing with.  
- **Kael**: Let's keep our eyes open.  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 street talk (`ch6_street_talk`)
> *You overheard a conversation at a cafe.*  
> *Two older trainers spoke in hushed tones.*  
- **Trainer A**: My cousin saw them in the old district.  
- **Trainer A**: Said they had matching robes. A broken hand symbol.  
- **Trainer B**: Sounds like trouble. What do they want?  
- **Trainer A**: Nobody knows. They just... watch.  
- **Kael**: *leaning back* Interesting.  
- **Lyra**: *whispering* Should we ask them more?  
- **\Player**: Not here. We'd draw attention.  
- **Kael**: The old district. Worth investigating later.  
> *You filed away the information for later.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 ragnar gym2 (`ch6_ragnar_gym2`)
> *As you approached the Gym, the doors burst open.*  
- **Ragnar**: TWO BADGES, BABY!  
> *Ragnar strutted out, his Pikachu sparking victoriously.*  
- **Ragnar**: Oh! \Player! You're just getting here?  
- **Ragnar**: HA! I'm still ahead!  
- **\Player**: *sighing* Hi, Ragnar.  
- **Lyra**: Is this your rival?  
- **Ragnar**: THE one and only!  
- **Ragnar**: Ragnar, future Champion, at your service!  
- **Kael**: ...Is he always like this?  
- **\Player**: Unfortunately.  
- **Ragnar**: You love it!  
- **Ragnar**: Anyway, good luck in there!  
- **Ragnar**: Spark's tough, but nothing compared to ME!  
> *He ran off, waving.*  
- **Lyra**: *giggling* He's fun!  
- **Kael**: That's one word for it.  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 gym2 building (`ch6_gym2_building`)
> *The Ashbury Gym specialized in Electric-types.*  
> *Its building crackled with visible energy.*

- **Lyra**: Still pretty!

- **Lyra**: Ready!  
- **Kael**: *nodding* Let's get this done.  
> *The Gym doors slid open automatically.*  
> *Inside, the hum of electricity filled the air.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 gym2 prep (`ch6_gym2_prep`)
> *The second Gym awaited.*  
> *But your mind was elsewhere.*

- **Lyra**: I know. It's a lot.

- **Kael**: The Gym. Then we investigate.  
- **Kael**: One thing at a time.  
- **\Player**: You're right. Let's do this.  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 gym2 leader intro (`ch6_gym2_leader_intro`)
> *The Gym Leader appeared in a flash of lightning.*  
> *A young man with spiky hair and an electric personality.*

- **Spark**: I heard that! But I'll forgive you...  
- **Spark**: If you can beat me in battle!  
- **\Player**: Bring it on!  
- **Spark**: That's the spirit! Luxray, let's go!  
> *The battle crackled with electric tension.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 gym2 victory (`ch6_gym2_victory`)
> *The battle ended with one final attack.*  
> *Spark's Pokémon fell, defeated.*  
- **Spark**: Whoa! You're stronger than you look!

- **Lyra**: Two badges! We're on a roll!

- **Spark**: I've seen some weird folks around town.  
- **Spark**: Hooded types. They give me the creeps.  
- **Spark**: Watch yourselves out there.  
- **Kael**: We've noticed them too.  
- **Spark**: Then be careful. Something's brewing.  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 being followed (`ch6_being_followed`)
> *After the Gym battle, you noticed them.*  
> *Hooded figures. Watching from the shadows.*  
- **Lyra**: *whispering* \Player... are those...?  
- **\Player**: *nodding* The Shattered Hand.  
- **Kael**: They've been following us for hours.  
- **Kael**: I counted three so far.  
- **Lyra**: Why are they watching US?  
- **Kael**: We found that tablet.  
- **Kael**: Maybe they noticed.  
- **\Player**: Should we confront them?  
- **Kael**: Not here. Too public.  
- **Kael**: Let's lead them somewhere isolated.  
- **Kael**: Then WE become the hunters.

> *You ventured into the old district.*  
> *Crumbling buildings. Empty streets. Shadows everywhere.*  
- **Lyra**: This place is creepy...  
- **Willow**: Vee... vee...  
- **Kael**: Perfect for a cult hideout.  
- **Kael**: Stay close. Watch for movement.  
> *You moved through the abandoned streets.*  
> *The feeling of being watched intensified.*  
- **\Player**: They're here. I can feel it.  
- **Kael**: Good. Let them come to us.  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 shadow encounter (`ch6_shadow_encounter`)
> *A figure stepped from the shadows.*  
> *Not attacking. Just observing.*

- **Hooded Figure**: The Chosen Ones should be protected...

- **Hooded Figure**: You'll understand soon.  
- **Hooded Figure**: When the marks awaken.  
> *They stepped back into the darkness and vanished.*  
- **\Player**: What marks? What's going on?!  
> *Silence was the only answer.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 6 regrouping (`ch6_regrouping`)

- **Lyra**: Chosen Ones. Marks. What does it all mean?

- **Kael**: Something connected to those guardians.

- **Kael**: I don't know. Yet.  
- **Kael**: But I intend to find out.  
- **Lyra**: Should we tell someone?  
- **Lyra**: Like Professor Aldric?  
- **\Player**: Good idea. He might know something.  
- **\Player**: Let's contact him tomorrow.

- **Marcus**: You will! Once I crush you in battle!  
- **Marcus**: I've already got two badges!  
- **Lyra**: So do we!  
- **Marcus**: Oho! Spirited one, aren't you?  
> *He winked at Lyra.*  
> *Kael's expression went cold.*  
- **Marcus**: Tell you what—let's battle!  
- **Marcus**: Winner gets bragging rights!  
- **\Player**: You're on.  
- **Marcus**: Not bad! But next time, I'll win!  
- **Marcus**: See you around, cuties!  
> *He waved and left.*  
- **Kael**: *muttering* I don't like him.  
- **Lyra**: *giggling* Is that jealousy?  
- **Kael**: No.  
- **Lyra**: Your ears are red.  
- **Kael**: They are NOT.
