### Chapter 7: First Confrontation - The Shattered Hand Attack

#### Scene: Chapter 7 road to professor (`ch7_road_to_professor`)
> *The road to Professor Aldric's lab wound through dense forest.*  
> *You'd been walking for hours.*  
- **Lyra**: *stretching* How much further?  
- **Kael**: According to the map, half a day.  
- **Lyra**: *groaning* My feet hurt!  
- **\Player**: We could camp soon.  
- **\Player**: It's getting dark anyway.  
- **Kael**: Agreed. I don't like traveling at night.  
- **Kael**: Too many unknowns.  
> *Shadow sniffed the air nervously.*  
- **Kael**: She senses something.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 forest journey (`ch7_forest_journey`)
> *The forest path was peaceful.*  
> *Too peaceful.*  
- **Lyra**: It's so pretty here!  
- **Lyra**: Look at all the Butterfree!  
- **Kael**: *scanning the trees* Something's wrong.  
- **Kael**: Where are all the other Pokémon?  
- **\Player**: You're right... it's too quiet.  
- **Lyra**: Maybe they're just—  
> *A rustling in the bushes.*  
> *Then another. And another.*  
- **Kael**: We're surrounded.  
- **Kael**: Those followers from the city.  
- **Kael**: They've been herding us here.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 trap realization (`ch7_trap_realization`)
> *You stopped in a clearing.*  
> *The path behind you was blocked.*  
- **Kael**: *cursing* I should have seen this.  
- **Kael**: They wanted us here.  
- **Lyra**: What do we do?!  
- **Willow**: Vee! Vee!  
- **\Player**: Stay calm. We fight if we have to.  
- **Kael**: Agreed. Back to back. Don't let them flank us.  
> *The three of you formed a triangle.*  
> *Your Pokémon at the ready.*  
> *Shadows moved between the trees.*  
> *Getting closer.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 ambush begins (`ch7_ambush_begins`)
> *Hooded figures stepped out from the trees.*  
> *Ten. Twenty. More appearing by the second.*  
- **Lyra**: *clutching Willow* There's so many!  
- **Willow**: Vee! Vee!  
- **Kael**: *drawing Shadow's Pokéball* Stay behind me.  
- **Shadow**: *materializing, growling*  
- **\Player**: *releasing starter* Let's take them together!  
- **Cultist**: Don't resist. This is inevitable.  
- **Cultist**: The Marked Ones must come with us.  
- **Kael**: Marked Ones? What marks?  
- **Cultist**: You'll understand soon enough.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 cultist battle (`ch7_cultist_battle`)
> *The cultists attacked!*  
> *Their Pokémon were dark and aggressive.*  
- **Cultist**: Mightyena, Shadow Ball!  
- **Cultist**: Sableye, Night Shade!  
> *Your team fought back desperately.*  
> *Shadow clashed with a Mightyena.*  
> *Willow dodged a barrage of attacks.*  
> *Your starter held the line.*  
- **Lyra**: There's too many of them!  
- **Kael**: Just hold on! Look for an opening!  
- **\Player**: There! The gap in their formation!  
- **\Player**: We can break through!  
- **Kael**: Together, on three!  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 ragnar rescue (`ch7_ragnar_rescue`)
> *Just as the cultists closed in—*  
- **Ragnar**: PIKA! THUNDERBOLT! NOW!  
> *A massive bolt of electricity struck the ground!*  
> *Cultists scattered, their Pokémon stunned.*  
- **Ragnar**: *landing from a tree* MISS ME?!  
- **\Player**: RAGNAR?!  
- **Ragnar**: Saw you heading into the forest!  
- **Ragnar**: Figured you'd get into trouble without me!  
> *His Pikachu sparked menacingly.*  
- **Ragnar**: Now who are these creepy hood guys?!  
- **Cultist**: Another one? Dispose of him!  
- **Ragnar**: HA! TRY IT!  
> *With Ragnar's help, the odds shifted.*  
> *You fought side by side, just like old times.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 vex arrives (`ch7_vex_arrives`)
> *The cultists parted.*  
> *A tall figure strode forward.*  
> *His presence made the air feel thick.*  
- **Vex**: Enough games.  
> *He removed his hood.*  
> *Sharp features. Eyes that gleamed with unsettling hunger.*  
- **Vex**: I am Vex, General of the Shattered Hand.  
- **Vex**: You three have been... difficult to locate.  
- **Lyra**: What do you want with us?!  
- **Vex**: *studying them* Fascinating.  
- **Vex**: You don't even know, do you?  
- **Vex**: The marks on your souls...  
- **Vex**: The guardians have chosen you.  
- **Kael**: Guardians? What guardians?  
- **Vex**: *smiling coldly* All in due time.  
- **Vex**: For now, I need to test something.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 shattered hand attack (`ch7_shattered_hand_attack`)
> *Vex raised his hand.*  
> *Dark energy crackled around him.*  
- **Vex**: The master wishes to see your potential.  
- **Vex**: Don't disappoint me.  
> *His Pokémon emerged—a fearsome Houndoom.*  
> *Flames licked its jaws.*  
- **Vex**: Let us begin!  
- **Vex**: Hmph. You have potential.  
- **Vex**: We will meet again, Chosen Ones.  
> *He vanished into the shadows.*  
- **Lyra**: What... was that about?  
- **Kael**: I don't know. But I intend to find out.  
- **\Player**: Whatever they're planning, we'll stop them. Together.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 cultists retreat (`ch7_cultists_retreat`)
> *With Vex's departure, the other cultists hesitated.*  
> *Then, as one, they melted back into the forest.*  
- **Lyra**: They're... leaving?  
- **Kael**: They got what they wanted.  
- **Kael**: Information. A measure of our strength.  
- **\Player**: This was just a test.  
- **Kael**: Exactly. Which means...  
- **Kael**: The real confrontation is still coming.  
> *The forest fell silent.*  
> *Only the sound of heavy breathing remained.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 aftermath (`ch7_aftermath`)
> *The cultists retreated into the shadows.*  
> *You stood in the clearing, shaken but alive.*  
- **Lyra**: *trembling* That was... intense.  
- **Willow**: Vee... vee...  
> *Lyra hugged Willow tightly.*  
- **Kael**: Chosen Ones. Marks. Guardians.  
- **Kael**: He knew things about us that WE don't know.  
- **\Player**: We need to find out what's going on.  
- **\Player**: Professor Aldric might know something.  
- **Kael**: Agreed. But first...  
> *He looked at Lyra with unexpected softness.*  
- **Kael**: Are you okay?  
- **Lyra**: *surprised* Y-yeah. I'm fine.  
- **Lyra**: Thanks for asking.  
- **Kael**: ...Don't get used to it.  
> *But he didn't move away.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 healing pokemon (`ch7_healing_pokemon`)
> *You tended to your injured Pokémon.*  
> *The battle had been fierce.*  
- **Lyra**: *applying potion* Poor Willow...  
- **Lyra**: You were so brave.  
- **Willow**: *weakly* Vee...  
- **Kael**: Shadow took some hits too.  
- **Kael**: But nothing serious.  
- **Shadow**: Zor...  
- **\Player**: *checking starter* You okay, buddy?  
> *Your Pokémon chirped affirmatively.*  
- **Lyra**: We make a good team.  
- **Lyra**: Even against those odds.  
- **Kael**: We were lucky.  
- **Kael**: Next time, we need to be prepared.  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 campfire setup (`ch7_campfire_setup`)
> *You set up camp in a safer location.*  
> *Away from the ambush site.*  
- **Kael**: I'll take first watch.  
- **Lyra**: Are you sure? You look tired.  
- **Kael**: I won't sleep anyway.  
- **Kael**: Too much to think about.  
- **\Player**: We'll rotate. No one stays up all night.  
> *The fire crackled softly.*  
> *Shadows danced at the edge of light.*  
> *But for now, you were safe.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 lyra fear (`ch7_lyra_fear`)
> *\\i[LYRA'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *That night, sleep wouldn't come.*  
> *Vex's words echoed in your mind.*  
- **Lyra**: (Chosen Ones... what does that even mean?)  
- **Lyra**: (I'm just a farm girl.)  
- **Lyra**: (I'm not special. I'm not brave.)  
> *Willow nuzzled against your leg.*  
- **Willow**: Vee...  
- **Lyra**: At least I have you, Willow.  
- **Lyra**: And \Player. And Kael.  
- **Lyra**: (Kael asked if I was okay...)  
- **Lyra**: (He never asks things like that.)  
- **Lyra**: (Maybe he's not as cold as he pretends.)  
> *A small smile crossed your face.*  
> *Whatever was coming...*  
> *At least you weren't alone.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 kael analysis (`ch7_kael_analysis`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *While the others slept, you analyzed.*  
> *Shadow lay at your feet, alert.*  
- **Kael**: (The Shattered Hand. A cult.)  
- **Kael**: (Connected to the shattered crowns legend.)  
- **Kael**: (They believe we're 'marked.')  
> *You looked at your arm.*  
> *Nothing visible. But something felt... different.*  
- **Kael**: (What if they're right?)  
- **Kael**: (What if I AM marked?)  
- **Kael**: (By what? For what?)  
> *Shadow whimpered.*  
- **Kael**: I know, girl. I don't like mysteries either.  
> *Your gaze drifted to Lyra's sleeping form.*  
- **Kael**: (She was scared today.)  
- **Kael**: (But she didn't run.)  
- **Kael**: (That's... admirable.)  
> *You looked away quickly.*  
- **Kael**: (Focus. We have work to do.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 player reflection (`ch7_player_reflection`)
> *\\i[\Player'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *Your watch came at the darkest hour.*  
> *The fire had burned low.*  
- **\Player**: (Chosen Ones. Guardians. Marks.)  
- **\Player**: (What have we stumbled into?)  
> *You looked at your sleeping friends.*  
> *Lyra, curled around Willow.*  
> *Kael, somehow still frowning in his sleep.*  
- **\Player**: (I'll protect them.)  
- **\Player**: (Whatever's coming...)  
- **\Player**: (We'll face it together.)  
> *Your starter stirred, sensing your mood.*  
> *It settled its head on your lap.*  
- **\Player**: Thanks, partner.  
- **\Player**: I'm glad you're with me.  
> *Dawn began to break on the horizon.*  
> *A new day. New challenges.*  
> *But you were ready.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 7 morning departure (`ch7_morning_departure`)
> *You broke camp as the sun rose.*  
> *The forest seemed less threatening in daylight.*  
- **Lyra**: *stretching* Morning, everyone!  
- **Kael**: *grunting* Coffee first. Talk later.  
- **\Player**: *laughing* Not a morning person?  
- **Kael**: Morning is an unnecessary invention.  
- **Lyra**: *giggling* Grumpy Kael is adorable.  
- **Kael**: I am NOT adorable.  
- **Lyra**: Sure you're not.  
> *The tension from last night faded.*  
> *You were still yourselves. Still friends.*  
- **\Player**: Let's move. Professor Aldric awaits.  
- **Kael**: Finally, someone with priorities.  
- **Lyra**: Hey! I have priorities too!  
- **Kael**: Breakfast isn't a priority.  
- **Lyra**: It absolutely IS!  
> *Laughing together, you continued your journey.*  


### Chapter 8: The Marks Appear - Complete Sequence

#### Scene: Chapter 8 peaceful night (`ch8_peaceful_night`)
> *The evening was calm.*  
> *You'd set up camp by a quiet stream.*  
- **Lyra**: *yawning* What a day...  
- **Kael**: At least no one attacked us today.  
- **Lyra**: Progress!  
- **\Player**: Let's get some rest. We're close to the professor's lab.  
> *The fire crackled softly.*  
> *Your Pokémon settled around you.*  
> *For a moment, everything felt normal.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 dream begins (`ch8_dream_begins`)
> *\\i[DREAM]*  
> *You floated in an endless void.*  
> *Light and shadow danced together.*  
> *Three massive figures appeared before you.*  
> *They radiated power beyond comprehension.*  
- **Voice**: Chosen One...  
- **Voice**: The time has come.  
- **Voice**: Receive our blessing.  
> *Light gathered around one of the figures.*  
> *It reached toward you.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 marks appear (`ch8_marks_appear`)
> *That night, the dream returned...*  
> *But this time, it was clearer.*  
> *Golden light. Three figures. Three crowns.*  
> *\\ts[]'Awaken, Chosen Ones...'*  
> *\\ts[]'The balance must be restored...'*  
> *\\ts[]'Before HE returns...'*  
> *You jolted awake, arm burning!*  
> *On your forearm... a faint symbol glowed.*  
> *Steel-blue light, pulsing like a heartbeat.*  
> *(What is this...?)*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 waking panic (`ch8_waking_panic`)
> *You scrambled to your feet, heart racing.*  
> *The mark on your arm glowed faintly.*  
- **\Player**: What... what is this?!  
> *Nearby, you heard Lyra scream.*  
> *And Kael's sharp intake of breath.*  
> *They were awake too.*  
> *They'd seen the same thing.*  
> *And on their arms...*  
> *Marks of their own.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 friends have marks (`ch8_friends_have_marks`)
> *You rushed to find Lyra and Kael.*  
> *They were already waiting, looking shaken.*  
- **Lyra**: You too...?  
> *She showed her arm. A rainbow-colored mark.*  
- **Kael**: ...  
> *He reluctantly revealed his. Dark crimson.*  
- **Lyra**: What's happening to us?  
- **Kael**: The cult mentioned marks.  
- **Kael**: Maybe this is what they meant.  
- **Lyra**: But what ARE they?  
- **Kael**: I don't know. But Professor Aldric might.  
- **\Player**: Then let's go find out. I'm not sitting around waiting for answers.  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 ragnar worried (`ch8_ragnar_worried`)
> *Before leaving to find Professor Aldric, Ragnar found you.*  
- **Ragnar**: Hey! There you are!  
> *He jogged over, then stopped dead.*  
- **Ragnar**: ...What's wrong?  
- **Ragnar**: You look like you've seen a ghost.  
- **\Player**: It's... complicated.  
- **Ragnar**: *crossing arms* That's what you always say.  
- **Ragnar**: But I know that face.  
- **Ragnar**: Something happened.  
> *You hesitated, then showed him your arm.*  
> *The mark glowed faintly.*  
- **Ragnar**: What the—?!  
- **Ragnar**: What IS that?!  
- **\Player**: We don't know yet.  
- **\Player**: That's why we're going to find answers.  
- **Ragnar**: ...  
- **Ragnar**: Okay. Be careful.  
- **Ragnar**: And call me if you need backup.  
- **\Player**: Since when are you so serious?  
- **Ragnar**: Since my rival got a glowing tattoo, apparently!  
> *Despite everything, you managed a small smile.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 comparing marks (`ch8_comparing_marks`)
> *The three of you sat together, studying each other's marks.*  
- **Lyra**: They're all different...  
- **Lyra**: Mine is rainbow, like a prism.  
- **Kael**: Mine is crimson. Dark red, almost black.  
- **\Player**: And mine is steel-blue.  
- **Lyra**: Three colors. Three of us.  
- **Lyra**: That can't be coincidence.  
- **Kael**: Nothing about this is coincidence.  
- **Kael**: The shared dreams. The cult knowing about us.  
- **Kael**: And now this.  
- **Lyra**: I'm scared...  
- **\Player**: Me too. But we're in this together.  
- **\Player**: Whatever these marks mean...  
- **\Player**: We'll figure it out as a team.  
- **Kael**: ...Agreed.  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 mark meanings (`ch8_mark_meanings`)
> *Kael studied the marks intensely.*  
- **Kael**: If I had to guess...  
- **Kael**: These correspond to the three guardians.  
- **Lyra**: The ones from the legends?  
- **Kael**: Exactly. Based on my research...  
- **Kael**: One guardian represented light. Connection. Life.  
- **Kael**: That would be your rainbow mark, Lyra.  
- **Lyra**: Oh...  
- **Kael**: Another represented shadow. Knowledge. Secrets.  
- **Kael**: *touching his crimson mark* That's mine.  
- **\Player**: And the third?  
- **Kael**: Will. Courage. The bridge between worlds.  
- **Kael**: Steel-blue. That's you.  
- **\Player**: So we're... connected to the guardians?  
- **Kael**: It seems so. The question is why.  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 marks react (`ch8_marks_react`)
> *When you placed your hands together...*  
> *Something unexpected happened.*  
> *The three marks pulsed in unison!*  
> *For a split second, you shared a vision.*  
> *\\i[Three thrones. Three crowns. Three guardians.]*  
> *\\i[And in the distance... a shadowy prison.]*  
- **Lyra**: Did you see that?!  
- **Kael**: Thrones... and something locked away.  
- **\Player**: It felt like a warning.  
- **Lyra**: What's in that prison?  
- **Kael**: I don't know.  
- **Kael**: But someone's trying to open it.  
> *The marks faded back to their normal glow.*  
> *But the image remained burned in your minds.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 pokemon reactions (`ch8_pokemon_reactions`)
> *Your Pokémon reacted strangely to the marks.*  
> *They could sense the change in you.*  
> *Willow sniffed Lyra's mark curiously.*  
- **Willow**: Vee? Vee vee?  
- **Lyra**: I don't know either, Willow.  
> *Shadow sat beside Kael, unnaturally still.*  
- **Shadow**: Zor...  
- **Kael**: She knows something's different.  
> *Your starter pressed against your leg.*  
> *Offering comfort. Offering support.*  
- **\Player**: At least they still trust us.  
- **Lyra**: They're our best friends.  
- **Lyra**: Of course they trust us.  
- **Kael**: *quietly* That's more than I've had before.  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 kael memory (`ch8_kael_memory`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *The crimson mark pulsed on your arm.*  
> *It reminded you of fire.*  
- **Kael**: (Fire. Always fire.)  
- **Kael**: (The orphanage. Mira.)  
> *Shadow whimpered, sensing your distress.*  
- **Kael**: (This mark... shadow and secrets.)  
- **Kael**: (The guardian of knowledge.)  
- **Kael**: (Maybe... I can learn what really happened.)  
- **Kael**: (Who started that fire.)  
- **Kael**: (Why Mira had to die.)  
> *Your fist clenched.*  
- **Kael**: (If this power can give me answers...)  
- **Kael**: (I'll use it.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 lyra hope (`ch8_lyra_hope`)
> *\\i[LYRA'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *The rainbow mark shimmered on your skin.*  
> *It felt warm. Almost comforting.*  
- **Lyra**: (Light and connection...)  
- **Lyra**: (That's what Kael said this represents.)  
> *You looked at your friends.*  
> *At \Player, who always stayed calm.*  
> *At Kael, who pretended not to care.*  
- **Lyra**: (Maybe this is why we found each other.)  
- **Lyra**: (Maybe we were meant to be a team.)  
> *Willow snuggled closer.*  
- **Willow**: Vee!  
- **Lyra**: *smiling* Yeah. We're going to be okay.  
- **Lyra**: (I believe that. I have to.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 player determination (`ch8_player_determination`)
> *\\i[\Player'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *You stared at the steel-blue mark.*  
> *Will. Courage. Bridge between worlds.*  
- **\Player**: (Why me?)  
- **\Player**: (I'm not special. I'm just...)  
> *You thought of your parents.*  
> *Dad, the former Champion.*  
> *Mom, who always believed in you.*  
- **\Player**: (They never gave up.)  
- **\Player**: (Neither will I.)  
> *Your starter nudged your hand.*  
> *As if to say: You're not alone.*  
- **\Player**: (That's right.)  
- **\Player**: (I have Lyra. I have Kael.)  
- **\Player**: (Together, we can handle anything.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 decision to continue (`ch8_decision_to_continue`)
> *That morning, you gathered your things.*  
> *The road ahead was uncertain.*  
- **Lyra**: So... we're really doing this?  
- **Lyra**: Going to the professor? Finding answers?  
- **Kael**: What's the alternative? Ignore it?  
- **Kael**: The cult won't stop looking for us.  
- **\Player**: And we can't run forever.  
- **\Player**: Better to know what we're dealing with.  
- **Lyra**: You're right. Both of you.  
- **Lyra**: I just... wish things could stay normal.  
- **Kael**: Normal was never an option for people like us.  
- **Lyra**: People like us?  
- **Kael**: Orphan. Farm girl. ...  
- **Kael**: We were never meant for ordinary lives.  
- **\Player**: Then let's make ours extraordinary.  
- **\Player**: Together.  
> *Willow and Shadow barked in agreement.*  
> *Your starter added its voice.*  
> *The team was ready.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 marks bond (`ch8_marks_bond`)
> *Before you left, something strange happened.*  
> *All three marks began to glow simultaneously.*  
- **Lyra**: Whoa!  
- **Kael**: Don't move. Let it happen.  
> *A warmth spread through your bodies.*  
> *For a moment, you could feel each other's emotions.*  
> *Lyra's fear—and her hope.*  
> *Kael's grief—and his determination.*  
> *Your own courage—and your doubt.*  
- **Lyra**: I felt... I felt both of you.  
- **Kael**: The marks link us somehow.  
- **\Player**: We really are connected.  
> *The glow faded, but the bond remained.*  
> *Whatever these marks meant...*  
> *You were in it together.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 departure scene (`ch8_departure_scene`)
> *The morning sun rose over the forest.*  
> *A new day. A new chapter.*  
- **Lyra**: Professor Aldric's lab is half a day away.  
- **Kael**: Then we should move.  
- **\Player**: Let's go get some answers.  
> *The three of you walked forward.*  
> *Marked. Changed. Connected.*  
> *Whatever destiny awaited...*  
> *You would meet it head-on.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 intro (`ch8_5_intro`)
> *\\i[INTERLUDE: KAEL'S NIGHTMARE]*  
> *\\i[The night the marks appeared...]*  
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *The others were asleep.*  
> *But you couldn't close your eyes.*  
> *Every time you tried...*  
> *You saw fire.*  
- **Kael**: (Not again. Not tonight.)  
> *Shadow stirred beside you.*  
- **Shadow**: Zor...?  
- **Kael**: It's nothing, girl. Go back to sleep.  
> *But she wouldn't.*  
> *She never did when the nightmares came.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 cant sleep (`ch8_5_cant_sleep`)
> *You walked away from the campsite.*  
> *Far enough that your movements wouldn't wake the others.*  
> *The new mark on your arm pulsed faintly.*  
> *Crimson. Like dying embers.*  
- **Kael**: (What does this even mean?)  
- **Kael**: (Death and secrets. Shadow and entropy.)  
- **Kael**: (Fitting, I suppose.)  
> *You stared at the stars.*  
> *Remembering another night.*  
> *Another sky.*  
> *And smoke that blotted out everything.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 memory begins (`ch8_5_memory_begins`)
> *\\i[MEMORY - The Orphanage]*  
> *\\i[Five years ago...]*  
> *You were eleven years old.*  
> *Small. Scared. Alone.*  
> *Except for Mira.*  
- **Young Kael**: Mira! Mira, where are you?!  
> *Smoke filled your lungs.*  
> *Flames licked at the walls.*  
> *The orphanage was burning.*  
- **Mira's Voice**: KAEL! Over here!  
> *You ran toward her voice.*  
> *Coughing. Choking. Terrified.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 mira found (`ch8_5_mira_found`)
> *Mira was trapped.*  
> *A beam had fallen across the doorway.*  
> *She couldn't get out.*  
- **Young Kael**: Mira! Hold on! I'll—  
- **Mira**: No, Kael. Listen to me.  
- **Mira**: The window. It's your only way out.  
- **Young Kael**: I'm not leaving you!  
- **Mira**: You HAVE to.  
- **Mira**: Please. You're the only one I can save.  
> *Tears streamed down your face.*  
> *The flames were getting closer.*  
- **Young Kael**: Mira... please...  
- **Mira**: I love you, little brother.  
- **Mira**: Now GO!  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 the push (`ch8_5_the_push`)
> *She pushed you toward the window.*  
> *With strength you didn't know she had.*  
- **Mira**: JUMP!  
> *You fell.*  
> *Through glass. Through fire.*  
> *Into the cold night air.*  
> *You hit the ground hard.*  
> *Looked back up at the window.*  
> *And saw Mira one last time.*  
> *Wreathed in flames.*  
> *Smiling.*  
- **Young Kael**: MIRA!!!  
> *The building collapsed.*  
> *And your sister was gone.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 aftermath (`ch8_5_aftermath`)
> *You woke up in a hospital.*  
> *Bandages on your arms. Ashes in your hair.*  
> *And a hole in your chest that would never heal.*  
- **Nurse**: You're awake. Oh, thank Arceus.  
- **Young Kael**: ...Mira?  
> *The nurse's face told you everything.*  
> *You didn't need to ask again.*  
- **Young Kael**: (She saved me.)  
- **Young Kael**: (She died... so I could live.)  
- **Young Kael**: (Why? Why her and not me?)  
> *From that day forward...*  
> *You stopped letting anyone close.*  
> *It was safer that way.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 finding shadow (`ch8_5_finding_shadow`)
> *\\i[MEMORY - One Year Later]*  
> *You were alone on the streets.*  
> *Scrounging for food. Stealing when necessary.*  
> *Trust no one. Rely on nothing.*  
> *That's when you found her.*  
> *A Zorua, beaten and abandoned.*  
> *Left in an alley to die.*  
- **Young Kael**: (Walk away. Don't get involved.)  
> *But something in her eyes...*  
> *Reminded you of Mira.*  
- **Young Kael**: ...Fine. Just this once.  
> *You carried her home.*  
> *Shared your meager food.*  
> *Nursed her back to health.*  
> *And when she woke up...*  
> *She refused to leave your side.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 shadow bond (`ch8_5_shadow_bond`)
- **Young Kael**: Don't get attached.  
- **Young Kael**: I'm not someone you want to follow.  
- **Zorua**: *tilts head* Zor?  
- **Young Kael**: I'm serious. People around me get hurt.  
- **Young Kael**: You should find someone else.  
- **Zorua**: *shakes head firmly*  
- **Zorua**: Zor. Zorua.  
> *She wouldn't budge.*  
> *No matter what you said.*  
> *No matter how cold you acted.*  
- **Young Kael**: (Stubborn thing.)  
- **Young Kael**: ...Fine. But I'm calling you Shadow.  
- **Young Kael**: Because that's all you're allowed to be.  
- **Shadow**: *happy bark*  
> *You pretended not to smile.*  
> *But she saw it anyway.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 back to present (`ch8_5_back_to_present`)
> *\\i[PRESENT - The Campsite]*  
> *You snapped back to reality.*  
> *The memories fading but never gone.*  
> *Shadow—no longer a Zorua—pressed against you.*  
- **Shadow**: Zor...  
- **Kael**: I know, girl. I know.  
> *Your mark pulsed again.*  
> *And for a moment...*  
> *You felt something else.*  
> *Not memory. Not pain.*  
> *Something... watching.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 yveltal first whisper (`ch8_5_yveltal_first_whisper`)
- **Voice**: (Child of entropy...)  
> *You spun around.*  
> *No one there.*  
- **Kael**: Who's there?!  
- **Voice**: (I am the ending. The necessary shadow.)  
- **Voice**: (And you... you carry my mark.)  
> *The mark flared crimson.*  
> *Pain shot through your arm.*  
- **Kael**: *gritting teeth* What do you want?  
- **Voice**: (To show you the truth.)  
- **Voice**: (About the fire. About your sister.)  
- **Voice**: (About why you were chosen.)  
> *Your heart stopped.*  
- **Kael**: You know... about the fire?  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 fire truth teased (`ch8_5_fire_truth_teased`)
- **Voice**: (I know all endings, child.)  
- **Voice**: (Every death. Every sacrifice.)  
- **Voice**: (Including hers.)  
- **Kael**: Then tell me! Who started the fire?!  
- **Voice**: (Patience.)  
- **Voice**: (When you are ready... you will learn.)  
- **Voice**: (But the truth may destroy you.)  
- **Kael**: I don't care.  
- **Voice**: (Good.)  
- **Voice**: (That determination... is why I chose you.)  
- **Voice**: (Face your trials. Master your grief.)  
- **Voice**: (And the answers will come.)  
> *The presence faded.*  
> *The mark stopped burning.*  
> *And you were alone again.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 lyra wakes (`ch8_5_lyra_wakes`)
- **Lyra**: Kael...?  
> *You turned sharply.*  
> *Lyra stood at the edge of camp.*  
> *Rubbing her eyes.*  
- **Lyra**: Are you okay? I heard you...  
- **Kael**: It's nothing. Go back to sleep.  
- **Lyra**: That's not what your face says.  
> *She walked closer.*  
> *Ignoring your obvious discomfort.*  
- **Lyra**: You can talk to me, you know.  
- **Lyra**: We're in this together now.  
- **Kael**: ...Why do you care?  
- **Lyra**: Because that's what friends do.  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 almost opening up (`ch8_5_almost_opening_up`)
> *You stared at her.*  
> *This strange girl with sunshine in her smile.*  
> *Who kept trying despite your walls.*  
- **Kael**: (Friends. When was the last time...?)  
- **Kael**: I had a sister once.  
- **Lyra**: ...  
- **Kael**: She died. In a fire.  
- **Kael**: She pushed me out a window and saved my life.  
- **Kael**: And I've never forgiven myself.  
- **Lyra**: Kael...  
- **Kael**: Don't. Don't say you're sorry.  
- **Kael**: Everyone says that. It doesn't help.  
- **Lyra**: ...Okay. I won't.  
- **Lyra**: But I'll be here. When you want to talk about it.  
> *You didn't know how to respond.*  
> *So you said nothing.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 lyra stays (`ch8_5_lyra_stays`)
> *Lyra sat down beside you.*  
> *Not too close. Not too far.*  
> *Just... present.*  
- **Lyra**: My mom died when I was little.  
- **Lyra**: I don't remember much about her.  
- **Lyra**: But I remember how much I loved her.  
- **Kael**: ...  
- **Lyra**: Loss doesn't go away.  
- **Lyra**: But carrying it alone makes it heavier.  
- **Kael**: You sound like a greeting card.  
- **Lyra**: *laughing* Maybe.  
- **Lyra**: But greeting cards exist for a reason.  
> *Despite yourself, you almost smiled.*  
> *Almost.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 pn joins (`ch8_5_pn_joins`)
> *Footsteps in the grass.*  
> *\Player walked toward you both.*  
> *Looking half-asleep but alert.*  
- **\Player**: Couldn't sleep either?  
- **Kael**: Why are you all awake?  
- **\Player**: My mark was burning.  
- **\Player**: Felt like something was watching me.  
- **Lyra**: Mine too.  
- **Lyra**: Is it... the Guardians?  
- **Kael**: Probably.  
- **Kael**: They're testing us. Or preparing us.  
- **Kael**: Either way, we're in for a rough ride.  
- **\Player**: Then we ride it together.  
> *You looked at them.*  
> *These two strangers who'd become something more.*  
> *And felt something you hadn't felt in years.*  
- **Kael**: (Hope. Dangerous thing.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 watchapter ing dawn (`ch8_5_watching_dawn`)
> *The three of you sat together.*  
> *Waiting for the sun.*  
> *Saying nothing. Needing nothing.*  
> *Shadow curled at your feet.*  
> *Willow nestled in Lyra's lap.*  
> *\Player's starter dozed against their leg.*  
- **Lyra**: Beautiful, isn't it?  
- **Lyra**: The sunrise?  
- **Kael**: ...Yeah.  
> *You'd forgotten what sunrises looked like.*  
> *For years, you only saw the darkness.*  
- **Kael**: (Maybe... it doesn't have to stay that way.)  
- **Kael**: (Maybe there's something after the night.)  
> *The sun broke the horizon.*  
> *Golden light flooded the world.*  
> *And for the first time in five years...*  
> *You felt warm.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 resolution (`ch8_5_resolution`)
- **Lyra**: *stretching* Ready to face the day?  
- **\Player**: Ready as we'll ever be.  
- **Kael**: Let's go.  
> *You stood.*  
> *Brushed the grass from your clothes.*  
> *And for just a moment, let your guard down.*  
- **Kael**: ...Thanks.  
- **Lyra**: For what?  
- **Kael**: For not running when you found out.  
- **Kael**: About me. About... everything.  
- **Lyra**: *smiling* Why would we run?  
- **Lyra**: We're marked together.  
- **Lyra**: That means something.  
- **\Player**: We've got your back, Kael.  
- **\Player**: Always.  
> *You nodded.*  
> *Not trusting your voice.*  
> *But meaning it anyway.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 8 5 ending (`ch8_5_ending`)
> *\\i[Kael's Nightmare - End]*  
> *\\i[The walls around his heart began to crack.]*  
> *\\i[Not broken. Not yet.]*  
> *\\i[But the light was getting in.]*  
> *\\i[Return to main story...]*  


## Act 2: AWAKENING (Chapters 9-18)


### Chapter 9: What Are We? - Seeking Answers

#### Scene: Chapter 9 journey to professor (`ch9_journey_to_professor`)
> *The road to Professor Aldric's laboratory was long.*  
> *Three days of walking. Three days of wondering.*  
- **Lyra**: I keep staring at my mark.  
- **Lyra**: Every time I look away, I have to look again.  
- **Kael**: Same.  
- **Kael**: It's like having a question burned into your skin.  
- **\Player**: At least we're getting answers soon.  
- **\Player**: Professor Aldric studies ancient history.  
- **\Player**: If anyone knows what these are, it's him.  
- **Lyra**: You trust him?  
- **\Player**: Dad does. They collaborated on research years ago.  
- **\Player**: Before Dad became Champion, he was a researcher too.  
- **Kael**: Wait—your father is Champion Marcus?  
- **Kael**: THE Marcus?  
- **\Player**: *sheepishly* I... don't like to bring it up.  
- **Lyra**: *jaw drops* Your dad is the CHAMPION?!  
- **Lyra**: Why didn't you tell us?!  
- **\Player**: I wanted you to like me for me.  
- **\Player**: Not for who my father is.  
- **Kael**: ...I can respect that.  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 campfire confessions (`ch9_campfire_confessions`)
> *That night, you camped under the stars.*  
> *The fire crackled softly.*  
- **Lyra**: So... Champion's kid, huh?  
- **Lyra**: That explains the expensive gear.

- **Kael**: My parents left me at an orphanage.  
- **Kael**: I don't know if they're alive or dead.  
- **Kael**: ...I tell myself I don't care.  
- **Lyra**: Kael...  
- **Kael**: It's fine. Ancient history.  
- **Kael**: Shadow's my family now.  
> *Shadow, as if understanding, curled tighter against his leg.*  
- **Lyra**: My dad left when I was six.  
- **Lyra**: Just... vanished one day.  
- **Lyra**: Elena—my sister—she basically raised me.  
- **\Player**: That must have been hard.  
- **Lyra**: It was. But Elena never complained.  
- **Lyra**: She always put me first.  
- **Lyra**: That's why I have to become strong.  
- **Lyra**: So I can protect her for once.  
> *The fire popped. Sparks drifted skyward.*  
> *Three marked strangers, bound by fate.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 ragnar splits (`ch9_ragnar_splits`)

- **Ragnar**: I'll be strong enough to matter.  
- **\Player**: Ragnar...

- **Ragnar**: I've got Gyms to conquer!  
- **Ragnar**: I'll see you at the League!  
> *He ran off with a wave.*  
> *That idiot. He really did care.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 lab arrival (`ch9_lab_arrival`)
> *Professor Aldric's laboratory sat atop a cliff.*  
> *Overlooking the sea. Isolated. Private.*  
- **Lab Assistant**: You must be the group Professor Aldric mentioned.  
- **Lab Assistant**: He's been expecting you.  
- **Lab Assistant**: ...Though I must say, you're all quite young.  
- **Kael**: Age is irrelevant.  
- **Kael**: Competence is what matters.  
- **Lab Assistant**: *flustered* R-Right this way.  
> *The laboratory was filled with artifacts.*  
> *Stone tablets. Ancient scrolls. Fossilized remnants.*  
- **Lyra**: *whispering* This place is amazing...  
> *An elderly man approached with warm eyes.*  
> *His coat was wrinkled. His glasses thick.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: Ah! Marcus's child!  
- **Professor Aldric**: You look just like your father did at your age.  
- **\Player**: Professor Aldric. Thank you for seeing us.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Thank ME? Child, you've brought me the discovery of a lifetime!  
- **Professor Aldric**: Now—show me these marks!  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 mark examination (`ch9_mark_examination`)
> *Professor Aldric studied the marks with fascination.*  
> *His instruments beeped and whirred.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: Remarkable... truly remarkable.  
- **Professor Aldric**: These symbols are ancient.  
- **Professor Aldric**: I've seen fragments in texts, but never...  
> *He adjusted his glasses, leaning closer.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: The energy readings are extraordinary.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Each mark pulses with a unique signature.  
- **\Player**: Do you know what they mean?  
- **Professor Aldric**: They appear to be... connection markers.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Bonds between humans and divine entities.  
- **Kael**: Divine entities?  
- **Professor Aldric**: Legendary Pokémon.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Or something even older.  
- **Lyra**: Older than Legendary Pokémon?  
- **Lyra**: What could possibly be older?  
- **Professor Aldric**: The Three Guardians.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Beings who existed before recorded history.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Legends say they were once human.  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 guardian researchapter  (`ch9_guardian_research`)
> *Professor Aldric led them to a room of scrolls.*  
> *Ancient texts from civilizations long forgotten.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: The Three Guardians appear across cultures.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Different names. Different forms.  
- **Professor Aldric**: But always three. Always together.  
> *He unrolled a fragile scroll.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: One of steel and valor—the Sword.  
- **Professor Aldric**: One of shadow and resolve—the Shield.  
- **Professor Aldric**: One of light and judgment—the Crown.  
- **Kael**: Sword... Shield... Crown.  
- **Kael**: Like a king's regalia.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Precisely! Some texts call them the Shattered Crown.  
- **Professor Aldric**: A single crown, broken into three pieces.  
- **Professor Aldric**: United, they could rule over all.  
- **Lyra**: The Shattered Hand...  
- **Lyra**: They want to reform the crown.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Which is why they hunt the marked.  
- **Professor Aldric**: You three may be the key to everything.  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 history lesson (`ch9_history_lesson`)
> *Professor Aldric spread a map across the table.*  
> *Ancient locations marked with faded ink.*  
- **Professor Aldric**: A thousand years ago, the Guardians walked among us.  
- **Professor Aldric**: They protected humanity from existential threats.

- **Professor Aldric**: War.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Humans wanted their power for themselves.  
- **Professor Aldric**: The Great Betrayal, some texts call it.  
- **Kael**: Humans betrayed the beings protecting them?  
- **Kael**: How predictable.  
- **Professor Aldric**: The Guardians were... wounded.  
- **Professor Aldric**: They sealed themselves away.  
- **Professor Aldric**: Waiting for humans worthy of their trust.  
- **Lyra**: And the marks...?  
- **Professor Aldric**: Signs that they've chosen again.  
- **Professor Aldric**: After a millennium of silence.  
- **Professor Aldric**: They've chosen the three of you.  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 summit temple direction (`ch9_summit_temple_direction`)
- **Lyra**: How do we learn more?  
- **Professor Aldric**: There are ancient texts in Mt. Corona.  
- **Professor Aldric**: At the Summit Temple.  
- **Professor Aldric**: If answers exist, they're there.

- **Professor Aldric**: They needed human partners.  
- **Professor Aldric**: The marked ones.

- **Professor Aldric**: The temple will reveal more.  
- **Professor Aldric**: But be warned—  
- **Professor Aldric**: The Shattered Hand knows of the temple too.  
- **Professor Aldric**: They will try to reach it before you.

- **Professor Aldric**: Your father trusted me, \Player.  
- **Professor Aldric**: And now I trust you.

#### Scene: Chapter 9 departure (`ch9_departure`)

> *Silent. Waiting. Patient.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 9 zacian first vision (`ch9_zacian_first_vision`)
> *\\i[DREAM - YOUR VISION]*  
> *You stood in a field of steel flowers.*  
> *Each petal sharp as a blade.*  
> *The sky was silver. The air tasted of iron.*  
> *Before you stood a wolf of living metal.*  
> *A sword rested in its mane, pulsing with power.*  
> *Its eyes burned with ancient wisdom.*  
- **Zacian**: So. You are the one who would bear my mark.  
- **\Player**: (I can't move... the pressure is overwhelming...)  
- **Zacian**: Fear is natural. Even I know fear.  
- **Zacian**: The fear of failing those I protect.  
- **Zacian**: But you did not run. You stood.  
> *The wolf circled you slowly.*  
> *Each step rang like a sword being drawn.*  
- **Zacian**: I was once human, you know.  
- **Zacian**: A warrior named Valdris.  
- **Zacian**: I gave everything to protect this world.

- **Zacian**: We became more than human to save what we loved.  
- **Zacian**: And in doing so... we lost what we loved.  
- **\Player**: That sounds... lonely.  
- **Zacian**: It is.  
- **Zacian**: A thousand years of loneliness.  
- **Zacian**: But now... perhaps...  
- **Zacian**: Will you make the same choice I made?  
- **Zacian**: To protect. To sacrifice. To stand.  
- **\Player**: Yes.  
- **Zacian**: We shall see.  
> *You woke with the taste of steel on your tongue.*  
> *Your mark pulsed brighter than before.*  
> *The mountain waited.*

### Chapter 10: The Mountain Path - Journey to the Summit Temple

#### Scene: Chapter 10 ragnar surprise (`ch10_ragnar_surprise`)
> *At the mountain base, a familiar voice echoed.*

> *Ragnar emerged from the nearby Pokémon Center.*  
> *His team looked battle-hardened now.*  
> *His Raichu's fur crackled with static.*  
- **\Player**: Ragnar? What are you doing here?

- **Ragnar**: I'm gonna catch it and add it to my team!  
- **Kael**: *muttering* Of course he is.  
- **Ragnar**: Hey Broody! Still traveling with \Player, huh?  
- **Kael**: ...My name is Kael.  
- **Ragnar**: Sure thing, Broody!  
- **Lyra**: *giggling* He's got you pegged.

- **\Player**: ...Three.  
- **Ragnar**: HA! I'm winning!  
- **Ragnar**: But hey, I heard some weird stuff is going on.

- **Ragnar**: You guys wouldn't know anything about that, right?

- **Ragnar**: *noticing* ...Right?

- **Ragnar**: *serious for once* ...Be careful up there, okay?  
- **Ragnar**: I've heard weird things about that mountain.  
- **\Player**: We will.  
- **Ragnar**: *grinning again* Good! Because I need my rival alive!  
- **Ragnar**: Can't beat you if you're dead!  
> *He waved and headed off on his own path.*  
- **Lyra**: He really cares about you, doesn't he?  
- **\Player**: In his own way... yeah.  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 mountain base (`ch10_mountain_base`)
> *Mt. Corona rose from the earth like a titan's fist.*  
> *Snow crowned its peak. Mist shrouded its slopes.*

- **Kael**: Two days of climbing. Maybe three.  
- **\Player**: Have you been here before?  
- **Kael**: No. But I know mountains.  
- **Kael**: The orphanage sat at the base of the Ironpeak Range.  
- **Kael**: I spent more time in those peaks than with people.  
- **Lyra**: That sounds lonely...  
- **Kael**: It was peaceful.  
- **Kael**: Mountains don't lie. Don't betray.  
- **Kael**: They just... are.  
- **\Player**: Well, we're not mountains.  
- **\Player**: But you can count on us too.  
> *Kael didn't respond.*  
> *But you caught a flicker of something in his eyes.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 first ascent (`ch10_first_ascent`)

> *Each step brought colder air.*

- **Kael**: The rocks are loose.  
- **Lyra**: *slips* Whoa—!  
> *Kael's hand shot out, catching her arm.*

- **Lyra**: *blushing* T-Thanks...  
- **\Player**: (He barely moved, but his reflexes are incredible.)  
- **Kael**: I'll lead. Step where I step.  
> *The three of you continued in single file.*  
> *Kael's movements were fluid, confident.*  
> *He truly was at home in the mountains.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 wild encounter (`ch10_wild_encounter`)

> *An Aggron emerged from a cave mouth.*

- **Kael**: It's protecting its territory.

- **Kael**: Shadow!  
> *Shadow leaped forward, meeting the charge.*  
> *The battle was brief but intense.*  
- **Kael**: *commanding* Foul Play!  
> *Shadow twisted, using the Aggron's momentum against it.*  
> *The metal beast stumbled back, surprised.*  
- **\Player**: It's backing down!  
> *The Aggron growled but retreated to its cave.*  
- **Lyra**: That was amazing, Kael!  
- **Kael**: Just survival.  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 mountain cave (`ch10_mountain_cave`)
> *A storm rolled in suddenly.*  
> *You took shelter in a shallow cave.*  
- **Lyra**: Where did this weather come from?!  
> *Wind howled outside. Snow fell in sheets.*  
- **Kael**: Mountain storms. They're unpredictable.  
- **Kael**: We wait it out.  
- **\Player**: At least the cave is dry.  
> *Your Pokémon huddled together for warmth.*  
> *Shadow sat apart, watching the storm.*  
- **Lyra**: Hey, Shadow.  
> *She sat down next to the Zorua.*  
- **Lyra**: You don't have to sit alone.  
> *Shadow looked at her, then at Kael.*  
> *Kael gave a slight nod.*  
> *The Zorua moved closer to the group.*  
- **\Player**: (Even Shadow is learning to trust.)  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 campfire bond (`ch10_campfire_bond`)
> *Night fell on the mountain.*  
> *The campfire crackled against the cold.*  
- **Lyra**: *shivering* It's freezing up here!  
> *Without a word, Kael removed his jacket.*  
> *He draped it over her shoulders.*  
- **Lyra**: *surprised* Kael...?  
- **Kael**: You were cold.  
- **Lyra**: But you'll—  
- **Kael**: I don't get cold.  
> *He was lying. You could see him shiver.*  
> *But Lyra just smiled and pulled the jacket tighter.*  
- **\Player**: (Something's definitely growing between those two.)  
- **Lyra**: Tell me something, Kael.  
- **Lyra**: Something about yourself.  
- **Kael**: ...  
- **Kael**: I grew up in an orphanage.  
- **Kael**: The mountains behind it were my escape.  
- **Lyra**: *softly* I'm sorry...  
- **Kael**: Don't be. It made me who I am.  
> *The fire crackled in comfortable silence.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 lyra opens up (`ch10_lyra_opens_up`)
- **Lyra**: I was scared of everything as a kid.  
- **Lyra**: The dark. Thunder. Being alone.  
- **Kael**: You don't seem scared now.  
- **Lyra**: Elena fixed that.  
- **Lyra**: She'd tell me stories to distract me.  
- **Lyra**: Hold me during storms.  
- **Lyra**: When Dad left... she became everything.  
- **Lyra**: Mom, Dad, sister—all in one.  
- **\Player**: She sounds amazing.  
- **Lyra**: She is. She really is.  
- **Lyra**: That's why I need to get stronger.  
- **Lyra**: So someday I can protect HER.  
- **Kael**: ...I understand.  
- **Kael**: Wanting to protect someone.  
> *His voice was quieter than usual.*  
> *Softer. Almost vulnerable.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 stargazing (`ch10_stargazing`)
> *The storm passed. The sky cleared.*  
> *Stars blazed above—brighter than any city.*  
- **Lyra**: *gasps* It's beautiful...  
- **\Player**: I've never seen so many stars.  
- **Kael**: In the mountains, there's no light pollution.  
- **Kael**: You see the sky as it truly is.  
> *He pointed to a constellation.*  
- **Kael**: That's the Three Guardians.  
- **Kael**: Or at least, that's what people used to call it.  
- **Lyra**: The same Guardians from the legends?  
- **Kael**: Probably.  
- **Kael**: Ancient peoples saw them everywhere.  
- **Kael**: In the stars. In the mountains. In themselves.  
- **\Player**: And now they're in us.  
> *Your marks pulsed softly.*  
> *Three lights among millions.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 kael memory flash (`ch10_kael_memory_flash`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *The mountain air triggered something.*  
> *A memory. Unbidden.*  
- **Mira's Voice**: Kael! Look at the view!  
- **Mira's Voice**: It's beautiful!  
- **Kael**: ...!  
- **Kael**: (Mira...)  
- **Lyra**: Kael? You okay?  
- **Kael**: ...Fine. Keep moving.  
- **Kael**: (She's been dead for years.)  
- **Kael**: (Why do I keep hearing her voice?)  
- **Kael**: (Is it the mark? These mountains?)  
> *Shadow nuzzled against his leg.*  
- **Kael**: *quietly* Thanks, Shadow.  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 mira memory (`ch10_mira_memory`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE - MEMORY]*  
> *Years ago. The orphanage rooftop.*  
> *A small girl with Kael's same dark hair.*  
- **Young Mira**: Kael! You have to see the sunset!  
- **Young Kael**: I've seen sunsets before.  
- **Young Mira**: Not like THIS one!  
> *She grabbed his hand and pulled him up.*  
> *The sky was ablaze—orange and pink and gold.*  
- **Young Mira**: See? It's magic!  
- **Young Kael**: *small smile* Yeah. It is.  
- **Young Mira**: Promise me something, Kael.  
- **Young Mira**: Promise we'll always watch sunsets together.  
- **Young Kael**: ...I promise.  
> *A promise he couldn't keep.*  
> *The fire had taken her three days later.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 ancient shrine (`ch10_ancient_shrine`)
> *High on the mountain, you found the shrine.*  
> *Weathered murals covered the walls.*  
- **Kael**: These are ancient. Thousands of years.  
- **Lyra**: Look! Three figures!  
> *She pointed to a faded painting.*  
> *Three silhouettes. Three crowns.*  
- **Kael**: The guardians...  
- **Kael**: But the details are too worn.  
- **Kael**: I can't make out their forms.  
- **\Player**: The temple should have more.  
- **\Player**: Let's keep going.  
> *As you passed the mural, your marks pulsed in unison.*  
> *Recognition. Connection. Something awakening.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 shrine inscription (`ch10_shrine_inscription`)
> *Kael studied an inscription below the mural.*  
> *His brow furrowed in concentration.*  
- **Lyra**: Can you read it?  
- **Kael**: It's ancient Coronan...  
- **Kael**: Similar to texts I studied.  
> *He traced the carved letters.*  
- **Kael**: 'Three who are one.'  
- **Kael**: 'Bound by fate, divided by form.'  
- **Kael**: 'When darkness rises, the marked shall stand.'  
- **\Player**: 'The marked shall stand.'  
- **\Player**: That's us.  
- **Kael**: There's more...  
- **Kael**: 'But beware the Fourth.'  
- **Kael**: 'The one who grasps but cannot hold.'  
- **Lyra**: The Fourth?  
- **Kael**: *darkly* Hoopa.  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 dangerous crossing (`ch10_dangerous_crossing`)
> *The path narrowed to a thin ledge.*  
> *A sheer drop fell away to the left.*  
- **Lyra**: I really, REALLY don't like heights.  
- **Kael**: Don't look down. Focus on my back.  
- **Kael**: One step at a time.  
- **\Player**: I've got you, Lyra. We'll go slow.  
> *Lyra pressed against the cliff face.*  
> *Her knuckles were white.*  
- **Kael**: You're doing well.  
- **Kael**: Just a little further.  
> *The ledge widened. Lyra collapsed against the rock.*  
- **Lyra**: Never. Again.  
- **Kael**: ...You did well.  
> *Coming from Kael, it was high praise.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 temple in sight (`ch10_temple_in_sight`)
> *As dawn broke, the temple appeared.*  
> *Stone spires reaching toward the sky.*  
> *Ancient. Majestic. Untouched by time.*  
- **Lyra**: *breathless* It's real...  
- **Kael**: The Summit Temple.  
- **Kael**: Built by the first vessels.  
- **Kael**: Or so the legends say.  
- **\Player**: We made it.  
> *The temple gates loomed before you.*  
> *Carved with the same three figures.*  
> *The Three Guardians.*  
- **Lyra**: Do we just... go in?  
> *As if in answer, your marks flared.*  
> *The gates began to open.*  
- **Kael**: I think that's our answer.  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 lyra guardian sense (`ch10_lyra_guardian_sense`)
> *\\i[LYRA'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *As the gates opened, warmth flooded through you.*  
> *Different from the cold mountain air.*  
- **Lyra**: (What is this feeling...?)

- **???**: Child of light.  
- **???**: You have come far.

- **Lyra**: A voice... calling me...  
- **???**: When you are ready, seek me.  
- **???**: In the light that judges all.  
> *The warmth faded, leaving only lingering hope.*  
- **Lyra**: I think... my Guardian spoke to me.  
- **Lyra**: For just a moment.  
> *Her mark glowed golden beneath her sleeve.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 10 entering temple (`ch10_entering_temple`)
> *You crossed the threshold together.*  
> *The temple swallowed you in shadow and stone.*  
- **Kael**: Stay alert.

- **Lyra**: *looking around* This place feels... alive.  
- **Lyra**: Like it's watching us.

- **Kael**: Ancient temples often have guardian spirits.  
- **\Player**: Comforting.  
> *The three of you ventured deeper.*  
> *Toward truth. Toward destiny.*  
> *Toward the First Revelation.*  


### Chapter 11: The First Truth - Summit Temple Revelations

#### Scene: Chapter 11 temple entrance (`ch11_temple_entrance`)
> *The Summit Temple rose from the mist.*  
> *Ancient. Massive. Humbling.*  
- **Lyra**: It's... incredible.  
- **Lyra**: I've never seen anything like it.  
- **Kael**: The architecture is pre-Pokémon League.  
- **Kael**: Older than recorded history.  
- **Kael**: The craftsmanship is... impossible.  
- **\Player**: Impossible how?  
- **Kael**: These stones are perfectly fitted.  
- **Kael**: No mortar. No tools could achieve this.  
- **Kael**: Unless the builders weren't... normal.  
- **\Player**: Let's see what's inside.  
> *The doors opened at your touch.*  
> *As if the temple had been waiting for you.*  
> *For centuries. For millennia.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 temple interior (`ch11_temple_interior`)
> *The interior was vast—impossibly so.*  
> *Larger inside than the temple's exterior suggested.*  
- **Lyra**: How is this possible?  
- **Lyra**: It seemed smaller from outside...  
- **Kael**: Space distortion.  
- **Kael**: The Guardians could manipulate reality itself.  
> *Murals lined every wall.*  
> *Depicting scenes of ancient glory and ancient sorrow.*  
- **\Player**: Look at these paintings...  
- **\Player**: They tell a story.  
- **Kael**: The history of the Guardians.  
- **Kael**: From their rise... to their fall.  
- **Lyra**: Why did they fall?  
- **Kael**: That's what we're here to find out.  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 first mural (`ch11_first_mural`)
> *The first mural showed three humans.*  
> *A warrior. A scholar. A healer.*  
- **Kael**: The original vessels.  
- **Kael**: Valdris, Moira, and... I can't make out the third name.  
- **Lyra**: They look so normal.  
- **Lyra**: Just people.  
- **Kael**: They were people.  
- **Kael**: Before they became Guardians.  
- **\Player**: Zacian told me—in my dream.  
- **\Player**: He was once a warrior named Valdris.  
- **Kael**: So it's true.  
- **Kael**: The Guardians were human.  
- **Lyra**: What changed them?  
- **Kael**: *pointing to the next mural* I think that did.  
> *The second mural showed darkness descending.*  
> *A formless horror consuming the world.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 nidhoggr mural (`ch11_nidhoggr_mural`)
- **Kael**: 'The Gnawing One. Nidhoggr.'  
- **Kael**: 'Before time. Before existence.'  
- **Kael**: 'Hunger given form.'  
> *The mural depicted a creature of pure chaos.*  
> *Writhing tentacles. Countless eyes. Endless maws.*  
- **Lyra**: *backing away* I don't want to look at that.  
- **\Player**: What is it?  
- **Kael**: The thing that nearly destroyed everything.  
- **Kael**: The reason the Guardians exist.  
> *The third mural showed the three humans transformed.*  
> *Wielding power beyond comprehension.*  
> *Driving back the darkness.*  
- **Kael**: 'They sacrificed their humanity.'  
- **Kael**: 'To seal the Gnawing One.'  
- **Kael**: 'They became something more.'  
- **Lyra**: *quietly* That's what we might have to do.  
- **Lyra**: Give up who we are.  
> *Silence hung heavy in the ancient hall.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 temple records (`ch11_temple_records`)
> *The inner sanctum held thousands of stone tablets.*  
> *Records of ages past.*  
- **Kael**: This will take months to translate...  
- **Lyra**: Wait! This one has pictures!  
> *She pointed to a large carved panel.*  
> *Three figures stood tall.*  
> *A wolf with a sword. A deer with rainbow antlers.*  
> *A bird of crimson darkness.*  
- **Kael**: The Guardians of Balance.  
- **Kael**: *reading* 'Protectors of the mortal realm.'  
- **Kael**: 'When chaos threatens, they choose champions.'  
- **Lyra**: Champions... like us?  
- **Kael**: *continuing* 'The Chosen Ones will bear their marks.'  
- **Kael**: 'And stand against the darkness.'  
- **\Player**: What darkness?  
- **Kael**: *frowning* 'A chaos entity of infinite hunger.'  
- **Kael**: 'It cannot be killed. Only sealed.'  
- **Kael**: 'And the seal is weakening.'  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 xerneas vision (`ch11_xerneas_vision`)
> *\\i[LYRA'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *Light exploded behind your eyes.*  
> *Golden. Warm. Overwhelming.*  
- **Lyra**: *gasps* What—  
> *You stood in a forest of crystal trees.*  
> *Each leaf reflected rainbow light.*  
> *Before you stood a deer of impossible beauty.*  
> *Antlers like rainbows. Eyes like stars.*  
- **Xerneas**: Lyra. Child of light.  
- **Lyra**: (I can't move... it's too beautiful...)  
- **Xerneas**: You fear the burden.  
- **Xerneas**: The weight of destiny.  
- **Lyra**: I... I'm scared I'm not enough.  
- **Xerneas**: I too was scared.  
- **Xerneas**: But love made me brave.  
- **Xerneas**: Love for those I protected.  
- **Xerneas**: Who do you love, child?  
- **Lyra**: ...My sister. My friends. My Pokémon.  
- **Xerneas**: Then you are already enough.  
> *The vision faded.*  
> *Lyra stood trembling, tears on her cheeks.*  
- **Kael**: Lyra? What happened?  
- **Lyra**: I... I saw her. Xerneas.  
- **Lyra**: She was... beautiful.  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 yveltal vision (`ch11_yveltal_vision`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *Darkness swallowed the world.*  
> *Cold. Absolute. Final.*  
- **Kael**: (What—)  
> *A bird of crimson and shadow materialized.*  
> *Wings that could blot out the sun.*  
> *Eyes of burning red.*  
- **Yveltal**: Kael. Bearer of shadows.  
- **Kael**: You're... the death Pokémon.  
- **Yveltal**: Death is not evil.  
- **Yveltal**: It is necessary.  
- **Yveltal**: I am the ending that makes new beginnings possible.  
- **Kael**: Why choose me?  
- **Yveltal**: Because you understand loss.  
- **Yveltal**: You have faced the void and survived.  
- **Kael**: ...Mira.  
- **Yveltal**: Your sister watches still.  
- **Yveltal**: From the other side.  
- **Yveltal**: She is proud of you.  
- **Kael**: *voice breaking* You're lying.  
- **Yveltal**: Death does not lie.  
- **Yveltal**: It is the only truth.  
> *Kael fell to his knees.*  
> *For the first time, tears streamed down his face.*  
> *Shadow pressed against him.*  
> *Lyra placed a hand on his shoulder.*  
> *He didn't push either of them away.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 hoopa revelation (`ch11_hoopa_revelation`)

- **Kael**: 'In the Divine Reckoning, it was sealed.'  
- **Kael**: 'But seals can break.'  
- **\Player**: The cult mentioned someone's 'return.'  
- **\Player**: They're trying to free this thing.  
- **Kael**: It gets worse.  
- **Kael**: 'The chaos entity is but a key.'  
- **Kael**: 'Behind it waits something older.'  
- **Kael**: 'The Gnawing One. Nidhoggr.'

- **Kael**: So Hoopa can free Nidhoggr.  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 seal tablets (`ch11_seal_tablets`)

- **Kael**: 'Power for power. Life for life.'  
> *Silence fell.*

- **Kael**: It means we might not all survive this.  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 burden of chapter oice (`ch11_burden_of_choice`)
> *The weight of those words settled over the group.*  
> *Heavy. Suffocating. Real.*

- **\Player**: Die to save the world?

- **Kael**: But the first vessels gave up their humanity.  
- **Kael**: We may have to give up something too.

- **Lyra**: Elena. Grandma.  
- **Kael**: And if the seal breaks?  
- **Kael**: There won't be anyone left to get back to.  
> *The truth hung between them.*  
> *Terrible. Unavoidable.*  
- **\Player**: We don't have to decide now.  
- **\Player**: We need more information.  
- **\Player**: And we need to stop the Hand first.  
- **Kael**: Agreed.  
- **Lyra**: *shakily* Agreed.  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 are we chapter osen (`ch11_are_we_chosen`)
> *You sat in the temple's main hall.*  
> *Processing everything you'd learned.*  
- **Lyra**: So... we're really Chosen Ones?  
- **Lyra**: Like in the legends?  
- **Kael**: The evidence suggests so.  
- **Kael**: The marks. The dreams. The cult's interest.  
- **\Player**: Can we refuse?  
- **Kael**: ...  
- **Kael**: I don't know.  
- **Lyra**: Do we WANT to refuse?  
> *Silence fell over the group.*  
- **\Player**: If we don't stop this...  
- **\Player**: Who will?  
- **Kael**: A fair point.  
- **Lyra**: Then... we do this.  
- **Lyra**: Together.  
- **Kael**: *small nod* Together.  
- **\Player**: Together.  
> *Your marks pulsed as one.*  
> *Acknowledgment. Acceptance.*  
> *The journey had truly begun.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 temple rumble (`ch11_temple_rumble`)
> *The temple shuddered.*  
> *Dust rained from the ceiling.*  
- **Kael**: *alert* That wasn't natural.  
- **Lyra**: Earthquake?  
- **Kael**: No. Listen.  
> *Distant sounds. Explosions. Shouting.*  
- **\Player**: Someone's attacking the temple!  
- **Kael**: The Shattered Hand.  
- **Kael**: They tracked us.  
- **Lyra**: What do we do?  
- **Kael**: We take the most important tablets.  
- **Kael**: Then we run.  
- **\Player**: We can fight!  
- **Kael**: Not their whole army. Not yet.  
- **Kael**: Live to fight another day.  
> *Another explosion rocked the temple.*  
> *Closer this time.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 gathering knowledge (`ch11_gathering_knowledge`)
> *You worked frantically.*  
> *Gathering smaller tablets. Memorizing murals.*  
- **Kael**: These describe the seal locations.  
- **Kael**: Where Hoopa is imprisoned.  
- **Lyra**: And this one shows how to strengthen it!  
- **\Player**: Take everything you can carry.  
> *Footsteps echoed in the outer halls.*  
> *The enemy was closing in.*  
- **Cultist Voice**: Spread out! They're here somewhere!  
- **Kael**: *quietly* Time to go.  
- **Lyra**: There's a back exit.  
- **Lyra**: I saw it in one of the murals!  
- **\Player**: Lead the way!  
> *The three of you slipped into the shadows.*  
> *Information secured. Lives intact.*  
> *For now.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 escape tunnel (`ch11_escape_tunnel`)
> *The back passage was narrow and dark.*  
> *Ancient stairs descending into the mountain.*  
- **Lyra**: *whispering* Watch your step. It's slippery.  
- **Kael**: Where does this lead?  
- **Lyra**: The mural showed it emerging near a river.  
- **Lyra**: On the mountain's far side.  
- **\Player**: Good. That puts distance between us and them.  
> *The sounds of the attack faded behind you.*  
> *But you didn't slow down.*  
- **Kael**: They'll realize we escaped.  
- **Kael**: They'll come after us.  
- **Lyra**: Then we'll be ready.  
- **Kael**: *glancing at her* Yes.  
- **Kael**: We will be.  
> *Light appeared ahead.*  
> *The tunnel's exit. Freedom.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 11 mountain escape (`ch11_mountain_escape`)
> *You emerged into cold mountain air.*  
> *The river roared below.*  
- **Lyra**: We made it!  
- **Kael**: Don't celebrate yet.  
- **Kael**: We need to put more distance—  
> *A figure stepped from behind a boulder.*  
> *Black cloak. Cold eyes. A general's bearing.*  
- **Shade**: Well, well.  
- **Shade**: The marked ones.  
- **\Player**: General Shade...  
- **Shade**: You've done well to find this place.  
- **Shade**: But the chase ends here.  
> *More cultists emerged from the rocks.*  
> *You were surrounded.*  


### Chapter 12: General Shade - First Confrontation

#### Scene: Chapter 12 surrounded (`ch12_surrounded`)
> *Cultists emerged from every direction.*  
> *Ten. Twenty. Too many to count.*  
- **Shade**: Did you really think we wouldn't find you?  
- **Shade**: The marked ones? Here?  
- **Shade**: Every spy we have was watching.  
- **Kael**: *through gritted teeth* We need to fight through.  
- **Lyra**: There are too many!  
- **\Player**: Then we make an opening.  
- **\Player**: Together.  
- **Shade**: How touching.  
- **Shade**: Surrender now, and I might let one of you live.  
- **Kael**: Counter-offer.  
- **Kael**: Leave now, and YOU might live.  
- **Shade**: *laughs coldly* Bold. I like that.  
- **Shade**: I'll remember your words when I'm carving them on your grave.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 shade reveal (`ch12_shade_reveal`)
> *General Shade stepped forward.*  
> *In the light, you saw her clearly.*  
> *Tall. Elegant. Terrifying.*  
> *Her cloak billowed despite the still air.*  
- **Shade**: I am Shade, General of the Shattered Hand.  
- **Shade**: First of Viktor's chosen.  
- **Shade**: And the one who will bring you to heel.  
- **\Player**: Viktor?  
- **Shade**: Our leader. The true heir to the crown.  
- **Shade**: When Hoopa is freed, he will wield its power.  
- **Shade**: And then... Nidhoggr.  
- **Kael**: You want to free the thing that nearly destroyed the world?  
- **Kael**: Are you insane?  
- **Shade**: Destroy? No.  
- **Shade**: Nidhoggr will remake it.  
- **Shade**: Burn away the corruption.  
- **Shade**: And from the ashes, paradise.  
- **Lyra**: That's insane!  
- **Shade**: Perhaps.  
- **Shade**: But insanity and vision are often mistaken for each other.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 shade backstory (`ch12_shade_backstory`)
- **Shade**: I was once like you, you know.  
- **Shade**: Young. Idealistic. Believing in heroes.  
- **\Player**: What happened?  
- **Shade**: The world showed me its true face.  
- **Shade**: My village was destroyed in a territorial war.  
- **Shade**: Pokémon against Pokémon. Humans caught in between.  
- **Shade**: My family. My friends. All gone.  
- **Shade**: While the 'heroes' watched from their towers.  
- **Kael**: So you joined the people causing more destruction?  
- **Shade**: I joined the people who will END destruction.  
- **Shade**: Nidhoggr's hunger will consume all conflict.  
- **Shade**: No more war. No more suffering.  
- **Shade**: Just... peace.  
- **Lyra**: The peace of the grave.  
- **Shade**: *smiles* You understand perfectly.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 battle begins (`ch12_battle_begins`)
- **Shade**: Enough talk.  
- **Shade**: Take them.  
> *Cultists surged forward.*  
> *Pokémon burst from Poké Balls in a wave.*  
- **Kael**: Shadow! Dark Pulse!  
> *Shadow's attack scattered the first wave.*  
> *But more kept coming.*  
- **Lyra**: Willow, support!  
- **Willow**: Vee!  
- **\Player**: Break through! Head for the path!  
> *You fought desperately.*  
> *For every cultist that fell, two more appeared.*  
- **Shade**: *watching calmly* Impressive stamina.  
- **Shade**: But futile.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 kael rage (`ch12_kael_rage`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *Rage burned through him.*  
> *Not at the cultists. At himself.*  
- **Kael**: (I led them here. My carelessness.)  
- **Kael**: (If they get hurt... it's my fault.)  
> *His mark began to glow.*  
> *Dark. Pulsing. Hungry.*  
- **Yveltal's Voice**: Use it.  
- **Yveltal's Voice**: Your anger. Your pain.  
- **Yveltal's Voice**: Let me help you.  
- **Kael**: *through gritted teeth* Not yet.  
- **Kael**: I don't trust you.  
- **Yveltal's Voice**: You trust nothing.  
- **Yveltal's Voice**: But you will.  
> *The mark's glow faded.*  
> *But the power lingered.*  
> *Waiting.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 lyra shield (`ch12_lyra_shield`)
> *\\i[LYRA'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *An attack came from behind.*  
> *Aimed at Kael's back.*  
- **Lyra**: NO!  
> *Her mark blazed golden.*  
> *Light erupted between Kael and the attack.*  
> *A barrier. Shimmering. Protective.*  
- **Kael**: *stunned* Lyra...?  
- **Lyra**: I... I don't know how I did that...  
- **Xerneas's Voice**: Instinct.  
- **Xerneas's Voice**: To protect those you love.  
> *The barrier flickered and faded.*  
> *But it had been enough.*  
- **Shade**: *eyes narrowing* Interesting.  
- **Shade**: The marks are awakening.  
- **Shade**: Good. Viktor will be pleased.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 player breakthrough (`ch12_player_breakthrough`)
> *\\i[YOUR PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *Your mark burned like fire.*  
> *Power surged through your veins.*  
- **Zacian's Voice**: Cut through.  
- **Zacian's Voice**: Like a sword. Like me.  
> *You raised your hand without thinking.*  
> *Energy gathered—steel-bright and sharp.*  
- **\Player**: MOVE!  
> *The energy released in a wave.*  
> *Cultists scattered before it.*  
> *A path opened through their ranks.*  
- **Kael**: GO! NOW!  
> *The three of you sprinted through the gap.*  
> *Shade watched you go.*  
> *She didn't pursue.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 shade lets them go (`ch12_shade_lets_them_go`)
- **Cultist**: General! They're escaping!  
- **Shade**: I know.  
- **Cultist**: Should we—  
- **Shade**: No.  
> *She watched the marked ones disappear into the mountains.*  
> *A thin smile crossed her face.*  
- **Shade**: Their marks awakened today.  
- **Shade**: We've learned what we needed.  
- **Shade**: Let them run.  
- **Cultist**: But Viktor ordered—  
- **Shade**: *coldly* Viktor ordered me to assess them.  
- **Shade**: I have.  
- **Shade**: They're stronger than expected.  
- **Shade**: But not strong enough.  
- **Shade**: The next time we meet...  
- **Shade**: Will be the last.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 escape run (`ch12_escape_run`)
> *You ran until your lungs burned.*  
> *Down the mountain. Through the forest.*  
- **Lyra**: *gasping* Are they... following?  
- **Kael**: *checking behind* No. They stopped.  
- **\Player**: Why? They had us.  
- **Kael**: Testing us.  
- **Kael**: She wanted to see our powers.  
- **Kael**: And we showed her.  
- **Lyra**: Was that... bad?  
- **Kael**: It means they know what we can do.  
- **Kael**: They'll be prepared next time.  
- **\Player**: Then we need to be more prepared.  
> *You finally stopped by a stream.*  
> *Safe. For now.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 catchapter ing breath (`ch12_catching_breath`)
> *The three of you collapsed by the water.*  
> *Exhausted. Shaken. Alive.*  
- **Lyra**: What... what happened back there?  
- **Lyra**: I made a shield. Of light.  
- **\Player**: I fired some kind of energy wave.  
- **Kael**: The marks. They responded to our need.  
- **Kael**: I felt it too. Yveltal's power.  
- **Kael**: I didn't use it... but I could have.  
- **Lyra**: It's scary...  
- **Lyra**: Having this power we don't understand.  
- **\Player**: We'll learn to control it.  
- **\Player**: We have to.  
- **Kael**: The tablets we took should help.  
- **Kael**: They describe the Guardians' abilities.  
- **Kael**: We can study them.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 what we learned (`ch12_what_we_learned`)
- **Kael**: We learned important things today.  
- **Kael**: About ourselves. About the enemy.  
- **Lyra**: Their leader is named Viktor.  
- **\Player**: And they don't just want Hoopa.  
- **\Player**: They want Nidhoggr too.  
- **Kael**: To remake the world through destruction.  
- **Kael**: Madness. Complete madness.  
- **Lyra**: But Shade believed it.  
- **Lyra**: Really believed.  
- **\Player**: That makes her more dangerous, not less.  
- **Kael**: Agreed.  
- **Kael**: A true believer will sacrifice anything.  
- **Kael**: Including themselves.  
- **Lyra**: So what do we do now?  
- **\Player**: We get stronger.  
- **\Player**: We find the seals.  
- **\Player**: And we stop them.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 shade aftermath (`ch12_shade_aftermath`)
> *As night fell, you made a simple camp.*  
> *No fire—too dangerous.*  
- **Lyra**: Is everyone okay?  
- **Kael**: We're fine. For now.  
- **\Player**: She said there's something worse than Hoopa.  
- **\Player**: 'Far greater,' she said.  
- **Kael**: The tablets mentioned Nidhoggr.  
- **Kael**: An ancient entity of chaos and hunger.  
- **Lyra**: So Hoopa is just the beginning?  
- **Kael**: It seems that way.  
- **\Player**: Then we need to stop them before they free either.  
- **\Player**: First, we regroup and recover.  
- **Kael**: And then?  
- **\Player**: And then we find the seals before they do.  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 night watchapter  (`ch12_night_watch`)
> *\\i[KAEL'S PERSPECTIVE]*  
> *You took first watch.*  
> *The others slept fitfully.*  
> *Shadow sat beside you.*  
> *Alert. Watchful. Loyal.*

- **Kael**: I won't become a monster.

- **Kael**: (They're counting on me.)  
- **Kael**: (I won't fail them.)  
> *The night passed slowly.*  
> *But it did pass.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 ragnar town (`ch12_ragnar_town`)
> *While restocking in a nearby town, a familiar voice called out.*  
- **Ragnar**: \Player! Is that you?!  
> *Ragnar jogged over, four badges gleaming on his jacket.*  
> *His Pikachu—no, Raichu now—bounded beside him.*  
- **\Player**: Ragnar! Your Pikachu evolved!  
- **Ragnar**: *proudly* YUP! We're unstoppable now!  
- **Ragnar**: Four badges and counting!  
> *He noticed your tired expression.*  
- **Ragnar**: ...You look rough, buddy.  
- **Ragnar**: Those dark times you mentioned?  
- **\Player**: Getting darker.  
- **Ragnar**: *serious for once* Look, I know I'm not part of  
- **Ragnar**: whatever weird chosen one stuff you've got going.  
- **Ragnar**: But if you EVER need backup—  
- **\Player**: I know.  
- **Ragnar**: Good! Now go get some rest!  
- **Ragnar**: You look like a Snorlax that hasn't slept in weeks!  
> *He ran off with a wave.*  
> *Annoying as ever. But it was nice to see him.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 12 dawn departure (`ch12_dawn_departure`)
> *Dawn brought cold clarity.*

- **Kael**: *almost smiling* Fair point.  
> *For a moment, despite everything...*  
> *Things felt almost normal.*  
> *Almost.*  


### Chapter 13: Growing Bonds - Recovery and Training

#### Scene: Chapter 13 recovery camp (`ch13_recovery_camp`)
> *You made camp by a river, far from the temple.*  
> *The night was peaceful. Almost too peaceful.*  
- **Lyra**: I made soup! Who's hungry?  
- **Willow**: Vee vee!  
- **Kael**: *quietly takes bowl* ...Thanks.  
- **\Player**: This is good, Lyra.  
- **Lyra**: *beaming* Grandma taught me!  
> *For a moment, you almost forgot the danger.*  
> *Almost.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 ragnar rematchapter  (`ch13_ragnar_rematch`)
> *While training on the route, a shout echoed across the field.*  
- **Ragnar**: HEY! BROODY! BATTLE TIME!  
> *Ragnar was already running toward you, Raichu sparking.*  
- **\Player**: Ragnar, I'm kind of busy—  
- **Ragnar**: TOO BAD!  
- **Ragnar**: You've been avoiding me for WEEKS!

- **Ragnar**: I HEARD THAT, DARK AND BROODY!  
> *The battle was intense.*  
> *Ragnar had gotten significantly stronger.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 ragnar after battle (`ch13_ragnar_after_battle`)

- **Ragnar**: That's MY job to annoy them!  
- **Lyra**: *laughing* We'll do our best!  
- **Kael**: ...Sure.  
- **Ragnar**: Alright! Next time, I WIN!  
> *He took off running again.*  
> *That boundless energy. It was almost inspiring.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 first night (`ch13_first_night`)
> *The fire crackled softly.*  
> *Above, stars emerged one by one.*  
- **Lyra**: Do you think the Shattered Hand is looking for us?

- **Kael**: But we're far from the temple now.  
- **Kael**: They won't find us easily.

- **\Player**: Put more distance between us.

- **Kael**: We study the tablets we took.  
- **Kael**: Find the seal locations.  
- **Kael**: And get there before they do.  
- **Lyra**: Right. We can do this.

- **Kael**: Wake me in three hours.  
> *The others settled into their bedrolls.*  
> *You watched the shadows.*  
> *Waiting.*  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 morning tablets (`ch13_morning_tablets`)
> *Morning brought the task of studying.*

- **Kael**: And one... the tablets don't say.  
- **Kael**: Just 'the place of falling stars.'  
- **\Player**: That's cryptic.  
- **Kael**: Ancient texts usually are.  
- **Lyra**: Which do we go to first?  
- **Kael**: Sunlight Forest is closest.  
- **Kael**: And it matches your Guardian, Lyra.  
- **Kael**: Xerneas was once called the Life-Giver.  
- **Lyra**: *touching her mark* Let's go there.  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 training montage (`ch13_training_montage`)

- **Lyra**: *laughs* That's Kael-speak for 'good job!'  

#### Scene: Chapter 13 kael trains player (`ch13_kael_trains_player`)
> *Kael approached you during a break.*

- **Kael**: Don't be.

#### Scene: Chapter 13 lyra helps player (`ch13_lyra_helps_player`)
